<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Yeah, size is no guarantee of power. Look at Ginny...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny's impressive <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Ginevra</b><sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <b>Molly</b><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> <b>"Ginny" Potter</b><sup id="cite_ref-PMQWC_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PMQWC-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> (née <b>Weasley</b>) (b. <a href="/wiki/11_August" title="11 August">11 August</a>, <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-DOB_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DOB-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> occasionally known as <b>Gin </b>by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CC_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-blood_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blood-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>, the youngest of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>'s <span class="template-c">(née Prewett)</span> seven children, and the first female to be born into the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley</a> line for several generations. She and her older brothers grew up in <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a> in <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>.
</p><p>Ginny attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> from <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>-<a href="/wiki/1999" title="1999">1999</a>, a year beneath the famous <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>. During her <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a>, she developed a long-standing crush on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and came under the influence of the memory of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>'s sixteen-year-old self. The memory was preserved in a <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">diary</a>, which forced Ginny to re-open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, endangering the lives of many students, including herself. Following that ordeal, Ginny grew into a confident young woman, becoming an important member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, an organisation taught and led by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in her fourth year. She would later fight in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> (<a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>), the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> (<a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>), and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> (<a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>). She was also an accomplished <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player, playing <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a> and <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> at different times for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ginny became a professional Quidditch player for the <a href="/wiki/Holyhead_Harpies" title="Holyhead Harpies">Holyhead Harpies</a>. Upon retiring from the Harpies, she became the senior Quidditch correspondent for the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>. Ginny eventually married Harry Potter and the couple had three children; <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a> (named after Harry's father and godfather), <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a> (named after <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna Potter</a> (named after Harry's mother and their friend <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>). By 2020, Ginny had become the sports editor for the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1981-1992)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281981-1992.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1981-1992)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1981-1992)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1981-1992)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Nine and three-quarters! Mum, can't I go...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Molly Weasley</b>: "<i>You're not old enough, Ginny, now be quiet.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ten year old Ginny's enthusiasm about attending Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Ginevra Molly Weasley was born on <a href="/wiki/11_August" title="11 August">11 August</a>, <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> (née <a href="/wiki/Prewett_family" title="Prewett family">Prewett</a>), the first girl born into the Weasley family in a long time, and the last for that generation after her six older brothers: <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>. At that time, the wizarding community she grew up in at the height of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, during which her maternal uncles, <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian Prewett</a>, were murdered while fighting a group of four <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>. The war eventually ended for a time two months later, after <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s first defeat <i>"at the hands"</i> of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">31 October</a>, <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20150828154152" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="168" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Burrow.png" data-image-key="The_Burrow.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150828154152" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20150828154152" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150828154152" decoding="async" width="250" height="168" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Burrow.png" data-image-key="The_Burrow.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150828154152" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Burrow.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Burrow, where Ginny grew up with her parents and six older brothers</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny and her six older brothers grew up in <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a> in <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. Despite the majority of her brothers being keen <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> players, Ginny wasn't allowed to play with them when she was a child. When she was six, she began a habit of breaking into the family broom shed and taking each of their brooms out in turn. She was never caught, and it only came to light eight years later when Hermione revealed it to Fred and George. 
</p><p>Ginny claims to have been looking forward to attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> ever since her eldest brother started at the school. Although as she would only have been a year old at the time, it is entirely possible that she was exaggerating here.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>Similarly, Ginny had always been shy around <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, when she had blushed and ran back to her room, and put her elbow in the butter dish.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180607010810" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry meeting the Weasleys..jpg" data-image-key="Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607010810" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180607010810" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607010810" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry meeting the Weasleys..jpg" data-image-key="Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607010810" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_meeting_the_Weasleys..jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Molly, Ginny, Ron, and Harry meet for the first time at King's Cross Station</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 1 September, 1991, Ginny accompanied her mother to <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a> to see off her brothers as they departed for Hogwarts. Despite being too young to attend the school, she still begged her mother to let her go with them. While saying goodbye to her brothers, she found out that Harry Potter was on the train, and tried to get her mother to let her go on the train to see him. As the train pulled out, she began to cry, despite her brothers promising to send her loads of owls and a Hogwarts toilet seat. She ran along the <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">platform</a> after the train, half-laughing and half-crying, then stopped to wave them off.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_8-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> returned to King's Cross in June 1992, Ginny was with her mother to welcome her brothers back and was again excited to see Harry, pointing him out to her mother as he came through the barrier between platforms nine and ten.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_8-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1992-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281992-1998.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1992-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1992-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1992-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_year">First year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>I d-didn't know! I found it inside one of the books <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Mum</a> got me. I th-thought someone had just left it there and forgotten about it!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny explaining how she got hold of the <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">diary</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125210110" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="311" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="COS promo Ginny Weasley T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary.jpg" data-image-key="COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle&#39;s_Diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190125210110" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125210110" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190125210110" decoding="async" width="250" height="311" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="COS promo Ginny Weasley T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary.jpg" data-image-key="COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle&#39;s_Diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190125210110" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her first year with Tom  Riddle's diary</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After seeing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> at King's Cross, Ginny developed feelings for him and talked about Harry all summer. When Harry arrived at the Burrow after being rescued from the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a> by <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>, she became extremely shy in his presence. On their first meeting, she came down for breakfast to find him sitting at the table. Startled, she retreated back to her room and stared at Harry as he passed her bedroom on his way to Ron's. Ginny became extremely clumsy around Harry and had a habit of knocking things over when he entered a room. On the day their <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_acceptance_letter" title="Hogwarts acceptance letter">Hogwarts letters</a> arrived, she blushed a deep red and knocked over a porridge bowl with a loud clatter and put her elbow in the butter dish when Harry asked her if she was starting at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny travelled to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> with her family to buy her school supplies, and her excitement at finally going to Hogwarts was tempered by the fact that, due to the Weasleys' financial situation, she would have to make do with a lot of second-hand products, including her robes and books. In <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a>, however, she became the owner of a brand new set of <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>'s collected works. Harry, having been given them by Lockhart as a publicity stunt, gave them to her since he could afford a set of his own and was embarrassed by what Lockhart had done. With this act of kindness and recognition, Ginny finally spoke in front of Harry, standing up to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> when he started to insult him.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Draco was with his father, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a>, and the elder Malfoy took the opportunity to insult the Weasley family for associating with the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> parents of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> witch <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and — in his eyes — being a disgrace to wizards. During his tirade, he managed to slip <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>'s <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">Diary</a> into Ginny's battered second-hand copy of <i><a href="/wiki/A_Beginner%27s_Guide_to_Transfiguration" title="A Beginner&#39;s Guide to Transfiguration">A Beginner's Guide to Transfiguration</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805182255" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805182255" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805182255" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805182255" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805182255" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-9236.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny confiding her feelings for Harry to Tom Riddle's Diary</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>Ginny started at Hogwarts on 1 September, 1992 and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>, like all the Weasleys before her. She discovered Tom Riddle's diary in amongst her school things and began writing in it. To her amazement, the diary wrote back, and she started to confide in Tom Riddle's memory, writing about how her brothers teased her, how she had to come to school with second-hand robes and books, and how she thought that Harry would never like her. She poured her heart out to the diary and told Tom's memory all about Harry's story. 
</p><p>At least once, Ginny went down toward <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>'s hut, hoping to see Harry there. In confiding in the diary her deepest fears and secrets Ginny became increasingly vulnerable to Tom Riddle's memory, which began to pour a little of his own soul back into her and slowly started to influence her.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> By the start of October, the signs of the influence began to show on Ginny. She started to look peaky, but a spate of colds in the school covered up the true nature of her condition. Her brother <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> forced her to take <a href="/wiki/Pepperup_Potion" title="Pepperup Potion">Pepperup Potion</a> to get her over it. By 31 October, the memory of Tom Riddle was able to take full control of Ginny and used her to open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, releasing its resident <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">Serpent of Slytherin</a> which then <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>'s cat, <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a> (whom she hung from a torch bracket) and put all the other students in great danger. Tom Riddle also forced her to write a threating message on the wall: "THE CHAMBER OF SECRETS HAS BEEN OPENED. ENEMIES OF THE HEIR, BEWARE."<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407011351" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginevra Weasley Writing on the Wall.gif" data-image-key="Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407011351" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginevra Weasley Writing on the Wall.gif" data-image-key="Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A possessed Ginny writing a message on the wall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the attack, Ginny seemed upset over Mrs Norris, and her brothers put it down to the fact that she was a cat-lover. She opened the Chamber of Secrets another two times, resulting in the petrification of <a href="/wiki/Colin_Creevey" title="Colin Creevey">Colin Creevey</a> and <a href="/wiki/Justin_Finch-Fletchley" title="Justin Finch-Fletchley">Justin Finch-Fletchley</a>. She became more visibly upset, and again, her brothers put it down to other causes — she sat next to Colin in <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a>, and that she was worried that Ron might be expelled if he got in trouble. Fred and George attempted to cheer her up, but went about it the wrong way by leaping out at her from behind statues covered in fur or boils.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny confided in the diary, however, that she thought she was going mad. She woke up with rooster feathers on her robes, and could not remember where she had been at <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en" title="Hallowe&#39;en">Hallowe'en</a> and when Colin was attacked. She started to think that she was attacking everyone.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> The missing pieces of her memory were starting to take a serious toll on her psyche and it was effecting her health beyond the point of looking peaky.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170529150328" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170529150328" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170529150328" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170529150328" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170529150328" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-16674.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny attempting to get rid of Tom Riddle's diary by flushing it down a toilet</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Along with her brothers, Ginny remained at Hogwarts over <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a>, instead of going to visit her brother Bill in Egypt with her parents. She had started to become suspicious of the diary, and several weeks after Christmas attempted to get rid of it by throwing it down a toilet in <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Moaning Myrtle</a>'s bathroom.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Once free of the diary, Ginny sent Harry an anonymous <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_Valentine_to_Harry_Potter" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s Valentine to Harry Potter">Singing Valentine</a> on <a href="/wiki/14_February" title="14 February">14 February</a>, <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>. He received it in front of her, as she was going into a Charms lesson, when he was accosted by the dwarf assigned to deliver it. During the delivery, Harry's bag was torn and the contents were dropped onto the floor. To Ginny's horror, she saw that Harry now had the diary. To make matters worse, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> implied that she had sent Harry the Singing Valentine in front of everyone.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny was fearful that Harry would discover her secrets, such as her feelings for him and how she thought he would never return her affections. In addition to the fact that she might be responsible for the attacks, so she waited until the boys' dormitory was empty. After the dormitory was empty for the day she then ransacked Harry's belongings to recover the diary. Retrieving it, Ginny was once more overcome by the memory of Tom Riddle and opened the Chamber again, this time petrifying Hermione Granger and <a href="/wiki/Penelope_Clearwater" title="Penelope Clearwater">Penelope Clearwater</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown how she felt about this, but it could be deduced that she most likely felt particularity upset about Hermione being petrified as she was a close friend of her brother and of her crush.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161211004513" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B2C17M1 Harry Ginny Tom Chamber of Secrets.jpg" data-image-key="B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211004513" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161211004513" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211004513" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B2C17M1 Harry Ginny Tom Chamber of Secrets.jpg" data-image-key="B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211004513" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B2C17M1_Harry_Ginny_Tom_Chamber_of_Secrets.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry with an unconscious Ginny lying in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny tried to tell Harry and Ron what was going on, but could not get the words out, and she was interrupted by Percy. The memory of Tom Riddle was furious, as he had been planning on taking on Harry Potter himself after learning his story. Realising that Harry would come to save Ginny, he made her write a farewell on a corridor wall, then enter the Chamber of Secrets to die. She had poured so much of her life into the diary that she could not fight Tom's control of her, and the last thing she remembered as she lay down on the floor of the Chamber was Tom coming out of the diary. The memory of Tom Riddle had fed off her, gaining enough strength to become corporeal and regain the appearance of his 16 year old self. As Tom grew stronger, the life in Ginny faded away until she slipped into an unconscious state.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Harry%26Ginny4.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140626013720" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&amp;Ginny4.gif" data-image-key="Harry&amp;Ginny4.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Harry%26Ginny4.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626013720" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Harry%26Ginny4.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140626013720" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Harry%26Ginny4.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626013720" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&amp;Ginny4.gif" data-image-key="Harry&amp;Ginny4.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Harry%26Ginny4.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626013720" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%26Ginny4.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny awake, explaining to Harry what happened</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny awoke in the Chamber to find that Harry had saved her, and destroyed Riddle's diary by piercing it with a basilisk fang, and Ginny's vitality was restored to her. Tearful and scared, Ginny revealed what had happened to Harry and was sure she was going to be expelled from school. After leaving the Chamber with the aid of the <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">phoenix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a>, Ginny was reunited with her parents in <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">McGonagall</a>'s office. Despite her fears, Dumbledore did not place the blame on her, saying that older and wiser wizards had been duped by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, and he sent her to the hospital wing to recover from her ordeal with a mug of hot chocolate.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following this traumatic experience, Ginny returned to normal and was happy and relaxed for the rest of the school term. At the end of the school year, she travelled back to King's Cross with her brothers, Harry, and Hermione on the Hogwarts Express, playing <a href="/wiki/Exploding_Snap" title="Exploding Snap">Exploding Snap</a>. She also mentioned that at some point she had walked in on Percy and Penelope Clearwater kissing in a classroom during the year, and begged her brothers not to tease him about it.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_year">Second year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Second year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>You want to set a good example to your sister!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Molly Weasley regarding the twin's antics<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170104011643" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170104011643" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170104011643" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny and her family in Egypt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny travelled to <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> in the summer of 1993 with the rest of her family to visit her brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> after her father won seven hundred <a href="/wiki/Galleon" title="Galleon">Galleons</a> in the annual <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet_Grand_Prize_Galleon_Draw" title="Daily Prophet Grand Prize Galleon Draw">Grand Prize Galleon Draw</a>. She visited various tombs, but her mother would not allow her to go in the last one because of all the mutant skeletons.<sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny and her family stayed at the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a> the night before setting off to start her second year at Hogwarts, and she met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> again. She was even more embarrassed in front of him than usual, muttering a hello but not looking at him. The next day, on <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">Platform 9¾</a>, she did meet his eyes as they shared a laugh over Percy's behaviour when trying to impress his girlfriend, Penelope.<sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the Hogwarts Express, Ginny was separated from her brothers until the train stopped because of the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>. In the dark, she found her way into the compartment containing Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a>. When the Dementors came to the compartment, Ginny was one of the worst affected by them as she had horrible experiences with Tom Riddle's diary last year. She went very pale and shook like mad, eventually sobbing and having to be comforted by Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later in the year, after Harry fell from his broomstick in a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match during a storm, Ginny visited him in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>. She had made him a get well card that sang shrilly when opened and presented it to him while blushing furiously.<sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_year">Third year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Third year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Third year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Right, this is getting stupid. Ginny, you can go with Harry, and I'll just —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>I can't, I'm going with — with Neville. He asked me when Hermione said no, and I thought... well... I'm not going to be able to go otherwise, I'm not in fourth year.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny misses her chance to go to the Yule Ball with Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170811220247" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-world cup.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170811220247" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170811220247" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170811220247" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-world cup.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170811220247" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-world_cup.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny at the 1994 Quidditch World cup with her friends and family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the summer of 1994, Ginny spent a lot of time with <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who was staying at the Burrow before and after the Quidditch World Cup. They shared Ginny's room and tent at the World Cup and solidified their growing friendship.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Aware of her interest in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, Hermione advised Ginny to relax around him more and show him what she was really like, since she could barely talk if he was in the same room as her. She even suggested that Ginny start going out with other available boys to mark time until Harry starts taking more notice and returns her feelings and becomes available.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Although she was still shy around Harry, who was also staying at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a>, Ginny took Hermione's advice and was much more relaxed and spent time with him, Ron, and Hermione. 
</p><p>She attended the Quidditch World Cup final on 25 August with the majority of her family, as well as Harry and Hermione. During the match she was shown wearing a green shamrock hat in support of the Irish. Ginny was shaken by the appearance of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in the aftermath of the Irish victory.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> During the riot Ginny's father put Fred and George in charge of her safety, while he and the elder Weasley brothers assisted the Ministry. She and the twins were separated from the trio and it was unknown where they hide while the trio was in the forest near the campsite. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140624035328" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="282" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="1962988 1330372913072 full.jpg" data-image-key="1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20140624035328" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140624035328" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20140624035328" decoding="async" width="175" height="282" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="1962988 1330372913072 full.jpg" data-image-key="1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20140624035328" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:1962988_1330372913072_full.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> dress robes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, which hosted the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> that year, she rooted for Harry the unexpected fourth champion and maintained a good relationship with Hermione. Ginny was the only one that Hermione confided in when <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> asked her to the Yule Ball. As a third year, Ginny was not allowed to attend the ball unless asked by an older student. <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> asked her to go after Hermione turned him down, having already accepted Viktor, and Ginny accepted since she was friends with him.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> She told Ron and Harry after <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> said Ginny should go with Harry.
</p><p>However, she still harboured feelings for Harry and was displeased to hear that he had asked <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a> to the ball. She was even more despondent when Ron suggested that Harry take her to the ball since he did not have a date. Struggling with the idea that she <i>could</i> have gone with Harry, she nevertheless remained loyal to her agreement with Neville and attended the ball with him.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> At the ball on <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a>, she met <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a> and started dating him at the end of the year.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_year">Fourth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fourth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Fourth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Cho Chang</b>: "<i>The Defence Association? The DA for short, so nobody knows what we're talking about?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Yeah, the DA's good. Only let's make it stand for Dumbledore's Army, because that's the Ministry's worst fear, isn't it?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny comes up with the name for the student defence group<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Tonks_morph.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140812154341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tonks morph.gif" data-image-key="Tonks_morph.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Tonks_morph.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140812154341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Tonks_morph.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140812154341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Tonks_morph.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140812154341" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tonks morph.gif" data-image-key="Tonks_morph.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Tonks_morph.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140812154341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tonks_morph.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny sitting next to <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> at 12 Grimmauld Place</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With the revelation that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> had returned in the summer of 1995, Ginny's parents became active members of the reconstituted <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. As a result, the family was relocated to the Order's headquarters at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12</a> <a href="/wiki/Grimmauld_Place" title="Grimmauld Place">Grimmauld Place</a> that summer. Ginny stayed at headquarters, sharing a room with Hermione, and helped her mother to clean the place to make it a suitable base of operations. She learned the truth about <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and met Nymphadora Tonks, who acted like a big sister towards her and Hermione. When Harry arrived at Number 12, Ginny was pleased to see Harry, and, due to her taking Hermione's advice and her relationship with <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, was relaxed and composed in his presence, showing none of the embarrassment and shyness towards him that she had shown during previous meetings.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to her age, Ginny was never allowed into Order meetings and when Sirius insisted on filling Harry in on the Order and Voldemort she was the only one banished from the meeting by her mother. However, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> &#8212; who was allowed to hear &#8212; told her everything anyway. When Harry was acquitted at his hearing on 12 August for using magic in front of a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> while under age, she was extremely pleased and sang and danced with Fred and George shouting "<em>He got off, he got off, he got off</em>...<i>!</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227211710" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP DA Ginny Reducto.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227211710" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227211710" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227211710" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP DA Ginny Reducto.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227211710" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_DA_Ginny_Reducto.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny casting the <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">Reductor Curse</a> during a D.A. meeting</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Ginny returned to Hogwarts on 1 September, 1995 with her brothers. During the train ride on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, Ginny introduced Harry and Neville to <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> in her year. With the arrival of new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> and a theory-based course, Harry, Ron, and Hermione decided to form a study group to teach practical defence spells. She joined the group, bringing her boyfriend Michael with her and several other Ravenclaws. They all met in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a> where Ginny first demonstrated her sense of humour by mimicking Umbridge's cough. During the first official meeting of the group, she came up with the name for the group — <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, which to her was a better name with the same initials of the name Harry's then-girlfriend <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a> came up with.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416124721" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="249" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190416124721" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416124721" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190416124721" decoding="async" width="249" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190416124721" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:GinnyExpectoPatronum.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny conjuring her Patronus</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During her time in the D.A, Ginny's talent for defensive magic was shown as she had swift reflexes with the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> and considerable power with the Reductor Curse, the latter of which highly impressed Harry (much to Ginny's delight) and made her brothers jealous. Toward the end of the fall of 1995, Harry, along with Fred and George, received a lifelong Quidditch ban from Umbridge for attacking <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> after their game against <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> (although their bans were lifted right after Umbridge was removed from Hogwarts). Ginny tried out for the team and became the new <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>. Although she admitted that Harry was a better Seeker than her, and that she preferred playing as a <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a> and scoring goals.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711140556" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys harry.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711140556" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys harry.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry informs the Weasleys of their father's attack at the Ministry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>What should have been a happy time for Ginny was marred by the attack on her father by <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> just prior to Christmas. Along with her brothers and Harry, she was instantly sent to 12 Grimmauld Place by a portkey to await news. Relieved to find out he was all right, Ginny saw him the next day in <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a> and hugged him immediately. Following the visit, she noticed that Harry started to distance himself from everyone, refusing to speak to anyone in the house. After Hermione skipped a skiing trip with her parents to come to the house, she talked Harry out of hiding in Buckbeak's room, leading him to Ginny and Ron. Learning that Harry had convinced himself that he had been possessed by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and attacked her father, Ginny railed on him for not seeking advice from the one person who had <i>definitely</i> been possessed by the Dark Lord. She quieted his fears by relaying her experiences to him and admitted that she had never truly gotten over it.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny spent Christmas at 12 Grimmauld Place and visited her father again on Christmas Day. During this visit, along with Ron and Hermione, she found out the truth about <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>'s parents, and how they had been tortured into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, Bellatrix, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a> using the Cruciatus Curse at the end of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Gina_weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090413023745" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gina weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Gina_weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Gina_weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090413023745" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Gina_weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090413023745" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Gina_weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090413023745" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gina weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Gina_weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Gina_weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090413023745" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gina_weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her Quidditch uniform before a match</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Returning to Hogwarts after Christmas, Ginny played her first game for the Gryffindor House team against <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>. Despite losing the match, Ginny captured the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Golden Snitch</a>, although she downplayed the achievement by saying it was not a fast Snitch and that the opposing Seeker, <a href="/wiki/Summerby" title="Summerby">Summerby</a>, had a cold. Probably as a result of her being more confident and relaxed in front of Harry, her willingness to stand up to him, and their shared experiences of being a Seeker, Harry and Ginny grew closer and became better friends.  
</p><p>The group name Ginny came up with for the D.A. eventually saved Harry from expulsion at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>'s hands when Cho's best friend <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a> betrayed the group to Umbridge, since the name gave Dumbledore a way to take the fall for the D.A.'s formation by reminding Minister <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> of saying that the group named themselves "<i>Dumbledore's Army, not Potter's</i>". This forced Dumbledore to then escape <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">the castle</a> with Fawkes' help in order to evade arrest, leaving Umbridge herself to replace him as <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">school head</a>. 
</p><p>Around Easter, Ginny had had her first real one on one conversation with Harry in the library, during which they ate Easter eggs together. When she persuaded him to talk to Cho (who had recently broken up with him in order to defend Marietta despite her treachery), Harry confided in her that he needed to speak to Sirius, and she encouraged him to do so, even insisting that she might be able to help. It's around this time that Ginny started to speak to Harry like a friend, and Harry in turn began to enjoy her company, although Ginny bringing chocolate into the library infuriated <a href="/wiki/Irma_Pince" title="Irma Pince">Madam Pince</a> to the point of violently chasing her and Harry out. Ginny then went to Fred and George, and asked them to find a way for Harry to speak with Sirius.
</p><p>In May, Ginny played her second game of Quidditch for the Gryffindor team against Ravenclaw. She managed to capture the Golden Snitch, beating Cho Chang and securing the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a> for Gryffindor. In the aftermath of the victory, Michael became very moody and sulked about the result. Because of his attitude, Ginny dumped him shortly after the match.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905041456" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge interrogating Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905041456" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905041456" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905041456" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge interrogating Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905041456" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_interrogating_Harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny and other D.A. members being held captive by Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry had a vision of Sirius being tortured in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a> by Voldemort on 18 June, he informed Ron and Hermione. The latter convinced Harry to check to see if Sirius was at 12 Grimmauld Place before rushing off to rescue him, and Ginny and Luna came to their assistance. With Harry and Hermione breaking into Umbridge's office, and Ron distracting her with news that <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> was wreaking havoc, Ginny and Luna stopped people from entering the corridor leading to the office by saying that someone had flooded it with <a href="/wiki/Garrotting_Gas" title="Garrotting Gas">Garrotting Gas</a>. Unfortunately for them, Umbridge saw through their ruse since she knew of Peeves's true location and ordered the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> to round them up. Ginny was captured by <a href="/wiki/Cassius_Warrington" title="Cassius Warrington">Cassius Warrington</a>, and when Neville saw what was happening and tried to help, he was caught as well. Ginny was restrained by a large sixth-year girl, though she was not an obedient captive and kept trying to break free by kicking her captor in the shins.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Umbridge threatened to use the Cruciatus Curse on Harry to make him tell her what he was doing, Hermione faked a breakdown and told a lie about a weapon that <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> had told them to make. She and Harry lured Umbridge into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>, leaving Ginny, Ron, Luna, and Neville alone with the Inquisitorial Squad. They managed to break free using skills that they had acquired in their D.A. sessions; Ginny personally dealt with <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, hitting him with her preferred <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a>. They then regrouped with Harry and Hermione, who had left Umbridge with a group of enraged <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP Death Chamber trio Ginny Neville Luna.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP Death Chamber trio Ginny Neville Luna.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny, Harry, Ron, Hermione, Neville, and Luna fight off Death Eaters in the <a href="/wiki/Hall_of_Prophecy" title="Hall of Prophecy">Hall of Prophecy</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Convinced that Sirius was in mortal danger, Harry resolved to travel to <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> and rescue him. Although Harry tried to prevent Ginny, Neville, and Luna from accompanying him, Ron and Hermione eventually persuaded him otherwise. After flying <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> to London, they entered the Ministry of Magic using the visitor's entrance and headed for the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>. In the Hall of Prophecy, they found no sign of Sirius, but Ron did find a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">prophecy</a> concerning Harry and Voldemort, but pertaining only to Harry. As Harry removed it from the shelf, the group was surrounded by Death Eaters led by <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> and learned that Voldemort had used the connection between himself and Harry to lure him there to remove the prophecy. Ginny was sadistically threatened with torture by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who wanted to use the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on her to force Harry to hand over the prophecy, thus hoping to avoid the inevitable fight that would break out.
</p><p>At Harry's signal, all six D.A. members fired <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">Reductor Curses</a> at the shelves to distract the Death Eaters and began running. Ginny, along with Luna and Ron, were separated from the other three and were chased through various rooms by Death Eaters. In one room containing a three-dimensional representation of the solar system, one of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> grabbed Ginny by the ankle. Luna used the Reductor Curse on a model of Pluto, causing it to explode in the Death Eater's face, but Ginny's ankle was broken in the process. 
</p>
