<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160226134828" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160226134828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160226134828" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160226134828" decoding="async" width="250" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160226134828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-13600.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny being threatened by <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">a Death Eater</a> in the Death Chamber</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Luna managed to get Ginny and Ron (who was also disabled) to safety, but Ginny's broken ankle immobilised her and restricted her ability to help in the battle. She grew distraught when Ron came under attack by the brains, and was knocked unconscious by a <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> to the face. Luckily, the Death Eaters were focused on the prophecy and Harry was able to lead them away from Ginny and the other vulnerable students. Ginny regained consciousness by the time Harry was pursuing <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, but he ignored her questions and raced past her.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the battle, Ginny recovered in the hospital wing at Hogwarts where <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> fixed her ankle in a trice. On the train ride back to London, Ginny revealed that she had ditched Michael, who had moved on to <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a> while Ginny had moved on to <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, much to Ron's horror.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She comforted Harry, who had lost his godfather, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> during the battle, when he was pushed right through the <a href="/wiki/Veil" title="Veil">veil</a>, the portal separating the world of the living from the world of the dead by his cousin, Bellatrix Lestrange.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_year">Fifth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fifth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Fifth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>I can't be involved with you anymore. We've got to stop seeing each other. We can't be together.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>It's for some stupid, noble reason, isn't it?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> uses people his enemies are close to... Think how much danger you'll be in if we keep this up. He'll know, he'll find out. He'll try and get to me through you.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry breaking up with Ginny for her own  safety<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210162837" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C6M1 inside Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes.jpg" data-image-key="B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys&#39;_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210162837" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210162837" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210162837" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C6M1 inside Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes.jpg" data-image-key="B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys&#39;_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210162837" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C6M1_inside_Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny with Molly and the trio  in Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny spent the summer of 1996 at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> with Harry, Ron, Hermione and the other Weasleys. Despite having to put up with her brother Bill's new fiancée, <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> (whom she nicknamed "<i>Phlegm</i>" and strongly disliked), she had a good summer practising Quidditch and planning to try out for the House team as a Chaser. With the summer holidays coming to a close Ginny, the trio, and some of the other Weasleys took a trip to Diagon Alley needed to purchase school supplies. While in Fred and George's new shop, <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a>, in Diagon Alley, she bought her first pet, a purple <a href="/wiki/Pygmy_Puff" title="Pygmy Puff">Pygmy Puff</a> that she named <a href="/wiki/Arnold" title="Arnold">Arnold</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>On 1 September, she met up with <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, but was interrupted by fellow D.A. member <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, who attempted to get information out of her regarding what had happened that night in the Department of Mysteries. Tired of his continued questioning, she cursed him with the <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a> and was seen by the new <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> master, <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>. Ginny feared detention, but Slughorn was so impressed with the hex that he invited her to take lunch with him as part of a select group of students he hoped to cultivate and induct into his Slug Club.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140623164230" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley playing Quidditch.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140623164230" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140623164230" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140623164230" decoding="async" width="245" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley playing Quidditch.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140623164230" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Weasley_playing_Quidditch.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny scoring a goal, while playing as a <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a> against Slytherin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As term started, Ginny tried out for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>, of which Harry had been made the Captain. She excelled as a Chaser and was given a spot on the roster. Following one Quidditch practice, she and Dean were caught kissing by Harry and Ron. She and Ron had a blazing argument over her kissing Dean in public, but Ginny countered that Ron only saw it as being wrong because he had never kissed anyone before. The argument led to a frosty relationship between the two siblings which lasted for quite some time.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the first Quidditch match of the season against <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, Ginny scored several goals to help the team to victory. Following the match, she purposely crashed her broomstick into the commentary box because the commentator, Zacharias Smith, had been making disparaging remarks about the Gryffindor team. Her feud with Ron over his attitude towards her and Dean was worsened when, in the aftermath of the victory, he began going out with <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, whom he often snogged in public. Ginny branded her brother a "<i>filthy hypocrite</i>" for his actions, but more or less seemed to be over the row they previously shared.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160904044458" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="GinnyWeasley WB F6 GinnyAtSlughornsParty Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160904044458" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160904044458" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160904044458" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="GinnyWeasley WB F6 GinnyAtSlughornsParty Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160904044458" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:GinnyWeasley_WB_F6_GinnyAtSlughornsParty_Still_080615_Land.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny arrives at Slughorn's Christmas party</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before the holiday break Ginny attended <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Slughorn's Christmas party</a> with Dean Thomas. She spent Christmas at the Burrow with her family and Harry, and when Ginny returned to Hogwarts, she seemed unenthusiastic about meeting up with Dean. After Ron was accidentally poisoned on his birthday, Ginny visited him in the hospital wing, and they seemingly forgave each other. She and Harry discussed what had happened to Ron endlessly, trying to come up with an explanation for what had happened.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny played in the Quidditch match against <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>, where Ron's bedridden status forced Harry to play the reserve Keeper <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>. During the match, McLaggen took one of the Beater's bats and pelted a Bludger directly at Harry. Harry was knocked unconscious and suffered a fractured skull. Dean, who had been playing as reserve Chaser in place of <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a>, laughed about the incident, causing him and Ginny to have a row. Ginny subsequently visited Harry in the hospital wing.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny and Dean were going through a rocky patch, and in April they finally split up when she accused Dean of always trying to help her through the portrait door into the Gryffindor common room. In reality, Harry had been wearing his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a> and bumped into her while under the influence of <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a>, but the incident finally brought an end to their already unstable relationship. Despite the break-up &#8212; or because of it &#8212; Ginny was still her usually bubbly self and hung around with Harry and Ron more because of Quidditch training. She also defended Harry's use of the <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse against <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, even if it had earned him a detention that forced him to miss the last Quidditch match of the year.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Harry%26Ginny.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140625205208" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&amp;Ginny.gif" data-image-key="Harry&amp;Ginny.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Harry%26Ginny.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140625205208" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Harry%26Ginny.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140625205208" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Harry%26Ginny.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140625205208" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&amp;Ginny.gif" data-image-key="Harry&amp;Ginny.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Harry%26Ginny.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140625205208" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%26Ginny.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Ginny's spontaneous first kiss</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Harry in detention, Ginny took the role of <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> for the Gryffindor team for the final match against Ravenclaw. They won the match and the Quidditch cup, and, during the post-match celebrations, Ginny and Harry spontaneously kissed. Ginny who had never really given up on Harry, was over the moon, as was he, as he had been harbouring feelings for her all year. Ginny and Harry started dating, although their time together was limited due to Harry's weekly detentions and Ginny's <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> reviews.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>On 30 June, <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> were let into the school by Draco Malfoy, while Dumbledore and Harry were away searching for one of Lord Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. Harry, who had suspected that Draco was a Death Eater for quite a while, forewarned Ron and Hermione to be vigilant and gave them the remains of his Felix Felicis potion. On Harry's orders Ginny joined Ron and Hermione in taking the potion, giving them extra luck in case they needed it. Along with Ron and Neville who had answered the D.A. call to arms, Ginny staked out the entrance to the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, which Harry believed that Draco was using for some unknown nefarious purpose. Later that night Harry was soon proven right.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Halfblood-04096.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155012" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Halfblood-04096.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-04096.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Halfblood-04096.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155012" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Halfblood-04096.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155012" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Halfblood-04096.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155012" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Halfblood-04096.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-04096.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Halfblood-04096.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155012" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Halfblood-04096.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny comforting Harry after the death of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They watched Draco emerge from the room with the <a href="/wiki/Hand_of_Glory" title="Hand of Glory">Hand of Glory</a>; when he saw them, he threw <a href="/wiki/Peruvian_Instant_Darkness_Powder" title="Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder">Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder</a>, blinding them and leading Death Eaters into Hogwarts via a <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Cabinet" title="Vanishing Cabinet">Vanishing Cabinet</a>. Fighting their way clear of the darkness, they met up with <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> and other members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> that were patrolling the school under orders from Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>  In the ensuing battle, Ginny duelled with <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a>, but suffered no injuries due in part to the Felix Felicis potion. In the aftermath, Ginny was shocked to find that her brother Bill had been badly injured and permanently scarred by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. She was able to lead Harry away from Dumbledore's corpse and up to the hospital wing, where Harry broke the news that Dumbledore had been killed by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. She seemed to accept Bill and Fleur's relationship after witnessing the love between them.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny sitting next to Harry at Dumbledore's funeral (left side, sixth row)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny took her <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>, despite the tragedy that had occurred at the school and spend most of her time with Harry. She attended Dumbledore's funeral, along with several others. At the funeral she sat next to Harry, Hermione, and Ron, instead of sitting with the rest of her family. After the former headmaster had been laid to rest, Harry broke up with Ginny. He feared that if <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> knew how he felt about her, she would become a target and he could not knowingly endanger her life. Despite saying that she knew the risks involved in being with Harry and that she didn't care, she accepted his decision, after he told her he would not be able to bear it if she died and it was his fault. She called his decision an act of stupid nobility.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sixth_year">Sixth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sixth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Sixth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>And then what does she thinks is going to happen? Someone else might kill off <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> while she's holding us here making vol-au-vents?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>So it's true? That's what you're trying to do?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A discussion of Harry's current plans<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180326174316" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180326174316" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180326174316" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180326174316" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180326174316" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-2067.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Molly and Ginny relieved at the safe arrival of Harry and Hagrid</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the death of Dumbledore, and the knowledge that the protective charm over Harry was due to end soon, as he would be turning 17 and legally an adult, The <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> arranged to move him from the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>' <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">home</a> to <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> on 27 July, via a plan that turned out to be highly dangerous. While most of her family went off to assist in the operation, which turned into a battle, Ginny stayed behind with her mother. As the team started to miss their <a href="/wiki/Portkey" title="Portkey">Portkeys</a>, Ginny started to worry for their safety and was only partially relieved to see Harry turn up at the Burrow. 
</p><p>She then explained that situation to Harry, stating that the other two-man teams were running late and that was why her mother was so worried. While waiting for the others to arrive she and Harry held hands, as a form of comfort and watching the sky silently. When <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> turned up with his ear cursed off, Ginny was shocked and helped her mother tend to him. Nothing could be done about George's missing ear, as it was cursed off by <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">dark magic</a>. Finally, as each member of her family returned, she allowed herself to relaxed, but the unexpected death of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">"Mad-Eye" Moody</a> greatly sobered the occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/Ginny%26Harry2.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140704022638" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny&amp;Harry2.gif" data-image-key="Ginny&amp;Harry2.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/Ginny%26Harry2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704022638" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/Ginny%26Harry2.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140704022638" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/Ginny%26Harry2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704022638" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny&amp;Harry2.gif" data-image-key="Ginny&amp;Harry2.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/Ginny%26Harry2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704022638" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny%26Harry2.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny kisses Harry at the Burrow as his seventeenth birthday present</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Over the next few days, Ginny interacted little with Harry because of their split, despite her feelings towards him. However, while setting the table for dinner Harry let slip that he, Ron, and Hermione were about to set off on a quest to stop <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. This caused Ginny to go pale and comment that she suspected that the trio's plans were something of the manner, considering Harry's drive to defeat Voldemort. Harry then tried to convince Ginny that he had spoken in haste and was just kidding, she did not believe it. 
</p><p>On <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_seventeenth_birthday" title="Harry Potter&#39;s seventeenth birthday">Harry's seventeenth birthday</a>, Ginny confessed that she did not know what to give Harry since anything she gave him would have to be small enough for him to carry around with him. Instead, she "<i>kissed him like she never had before</i>" in the hopes of giving him something to remember her by. She did this in case he met someone else on his travels, something he assured her would be unlikely to happen. Ginny felt comforted by this and viewed it as the silver lining she had been looking for. However, they were interrupted by a disapproving <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, with Hermione in tow.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> As Harry exited her bedroom it was mentioned that Ginny might have for once finally succumb to tears.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180531205912" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wedding Ginny&amp;Ron.jpg" data-image-key="Wedding_Ginny&amp;Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180531205912" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180531205912" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180531205912" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wedding Ginny&amp;Ron.jpg" data-image-key="Wedding_Ginny&amp;Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180531205912" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wedding_Ginny%26Ron.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny talking to Ron at <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_Fleur_Delacour_and_Bill_Weasley" class="mw-redirect" title="Wedding of Fleur Delacour and Bill Weasley">Bill and Fleur's wedding</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 1 August Ginny served as a bridesmaid at Bill and Fleur's wedding, along with <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Delacour" title="Gabrielle Delacour">Gabrielle Delacour</a>. When Gabrielle batted her eyelashes at Harry, Ginny coughed loudly to indicate her annoyance. She wore a golden dress and as the ceremony began, her <a href="/wiki/Muriel" title="Muriel">Auntie Muriel</a> remarked in a carrying whisper that her dress was far too low cut. Ginny responded to this by turning around and winking at Harry. During the reception, she danced with <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a>, and others. Harry (disguised as a member of the Weasley family) jealously warned <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> off of speaking with her, when he remarked on Ginny's attractiveness. He warned him that she had a big and jealous boyfriend. 
</p><p>In the middle of the celebration, the guests were warned by <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> that the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> had fallen, that <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> was dead, and that the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> were coming. As the Death Eaters stormed the wedding, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> apparated herself, Harry, and Ron away from the chaos to begin their <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> quest. Ginny was seen defending herself against a Death Eater and was unable to say goodbye to Harry and the two did not see each other again for almost a year. The Weasley family was questioned, but none of them were harmed.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110407195913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Death Eaters inside Hogwarts Express 02.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110407195913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110407195913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110407195913" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Death Eaters inside Hogwarts Express 02.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110407195913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Death_Eaters_inside_Hogwarts_Express_02.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny and others, Death Eaters storm the Hogwarts Express in search of Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As part of the new Ministry's regime, Hogwarts attendance became mandatory and <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a> were being rounded up. Ginny was present on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> on 1 September 1997 when it was raided by three Death Eaters in search of Harry Potter. Once at school, Ginny joined up with <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> and Luna Lovegood to restart the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> and defy Snape's regime. They openly defied authority and snuck out at night painting graffiti on the walls of the corridors — "<i>Dumbledore's Army, still recruiting"</i>. On one occasion, they attempted to steal <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a> from Snape's office because they had knowledge that Harry needed it, but were caught and punished. Ginny served detention with <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and was banned from all trips to <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>. Ginny and Neville were left to lead the D.A. without Luna after she was abducted by Death Eaters over the Christmas holidays.
</p><p>During the Easter holidays, Ginny was at the Burrow when the Weasleys were forced into hiding at Aunt Muriel's after Ron's accompaniment of Harry and Hermione was discovered by the Death Eaters.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Harry turned and saw Ginny and Tonks, both with their wand drawn at the next window, which was missing several panes. Even as he watched, Ginny sent a well aimed <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinx</a> into the crowd of fighters below.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny fighting in the opening stage of the final battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>When Harry, Hermione, and Ron returned to Hogwarts on 1 May, 1998 in search of a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, they were met by Neville and the remnants of Dumbledore's Army that had stood up to Snape and the Carrows. Acting on a promise to Ginny, Neville sent word to her that Harry was at the school. Ginny arrived with her brothers, <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>. They arrived on the understanding that a battle was about to be fought.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> She was incredibly relieved to see the trio, particularly Harry and expressed her displeasure at Cho's lingering feelings for him. Cho's eagerness to escort Harry to Ravenclaw Tower irritated her and in turn insisted that her friend <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> do it instead.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Da_On_the_bridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811142125" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Da On the bridge.jpg" data-image-key="Da_On_the_bridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Da_On_the_bridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811142125" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Da_On_the_bridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811142125" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Da_On_the_bridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811142125" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Da On the bridge.jpg" data-image-key="Da_On_the_bridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Da_On_the_bridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811142125" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Da_On_the_bridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny and the other <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> members preparing to blow up the covered bridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As more members of Dumbledore's Army and the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> arrived for battle, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Mr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Mrs Weasley</a> forbade their daughter to take part in the fighting, since she was underage. Ginny furiously argued against it, as it was hypocritical, since Harry was much younger than her when he faced Voldemort all the previous times. Also, she did not want to leave when her whole family and Harry would be fighting and wait at home for news. <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> offered a compromise: Ginny would stay in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> so as to be on the scene, but would not involve herself in the fighting. Although she did not like it, she grudgingly agreed.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> She proceeded to stay in the room.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Weasley_dh2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911013129" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley dh2.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_dh2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Weasley_dh2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911013129" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Weasley_dh2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911013129" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Weasley_dh2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911013129" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley dh2.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_dh2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Weasley_dh2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911013129" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_dh2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny mourning with her family during the One-hour armistice</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 2 May during the battle, Harry needed the Room of Requirement to change form into the Room of Hidden Things, in order to retrieve one of Voldemort's Horcruxes, <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Diadem</a>. He asked Ginny to leave the room, on the proviso that she would re-enter it once he had completed his task, not believing that she would. Freed of her sanctuary Ginny joined the battle with a flourish. She and <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> were later seen by Harry firing well aimed jinxes from a high-up window into the crowd of fighters below.
</p><p>After the initial fighting <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> called a temporary truce to allow the combatants to retrieve their dead, and for Harry to give himself up to avoid further killing. Ginny was shocked and heartbroken by the death of her brother <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, and was comforted by Hermione. She later assisted in the recovery of the wounded outside the castle. When Harry passed her on his way to face Voldemort in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> under the <a href="/wiki/Invisibility_cloak" title="Invisibility cloak">Invisibility cloak</a>, she was comforting an injured girl. Harry thought she might have sensed his presence as he walked away, but the two had no contact, as Harry did not want anyone to try and stop him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227213745" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH2 Ginny blocking Bellatrix.gif" data-image-key="DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227213745" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227213745" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227213745" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH2 Ginny blocking Bellatrix.gif" data-image-key="DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227213745" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH2_Ginny_blocking_Bellatrix.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny is spared death at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> by mere inches</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the seemingly lifeless body of Harry was presented to the defenders of Hogwarts by Voldemort, Ginny let out a terrible scream of anger, grief and denial that was terrible to hear. However, his apparent death spurred the defenders on, and Neville took up the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> and beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>. With the battle restarted Ginny, Luna, and Hermione duelled Bellatrix Lestrange, the last Death Eater at that point still standing. Bellatrix was more than a match for the three, however, and fired a <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> that missed Ginny by an inch. Witnessed by both her mother and Harry, the action spurred both of them to charge the Death Eater. Molly got there first and after a fantastically vicious duel, Lestrange fell to the floor stone dead. Ginny witnessed Harry's final defeat of Lord Voldemort, and was one of the first people to run and hug him. She sat with her head on her mother's shoulder during the victory celebrations in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Later_life_(1998-2020)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Later_life_.281998-2020.29">Later life <span class="template-c">(1998-2020)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-2020)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-2020)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Accio Quote!">"<i>Ginny Weasley, stuck with her athletic career, playing for the <a href="/wiki/Holyhead_Harpies" title="Holyhead Harpies">Holyhead Harpies</a>, the all-female Quidditch team. Eventually, Ginny left the team to raise their three children — James, Albus, and Lily — while writing as the senior Quidditch correspondent for the wizarding newspaper, the Daily Prophet.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> regarding Ginny's life in the future<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Accio_Quote!" title="Accio Quote!">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ginny and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> rekindled their passionate romance. For several years Ginny was part of the Quidditch team, the Holyhead Harpies.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_21-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> At some point she and Harry were married and her last name became Potter. She eventually retired and the couple had a family. She gave birth to three children: <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Ginny later became the senior <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> correspondent for the <i>Daily Prophet</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_21-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811150508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811150508" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811150508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A 36 year old Ginny Potter with her family in <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In her capacity as Quidditch correspondent Ginny attended the <a href="/wiki/2014_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="2014 Quidditch World Cup">2014 Quidditch World Cup</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Patagonian_Desert" title="Patagonian Desert">Patagonian Desert</a>. While here, she wrote several articles for the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> using her married name, Ginny Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Her family joined her to watch the finals of the Cup in July<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>. Ginny covered the outcome of the Brazil vs Bulgaria match live along with <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>. The latter while in the journalists' enclosure repeatedly made corrections to Ginny's reports. This continued until shortly after the match ended, Rita remarked that her husband Harry Potter was "<i>publicity-hungry</i>" — just as Ginny was approaching. That last remark sailed a bit too close to home and Rita was taken "unaccountably ill" with what some called "<i>a jinx to the solar plexus</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-the-qwc2014-final_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-the-qwc2014-final-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a>, <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Harry and Ginny escorted their children James and Albus to the Hogwarts Express, where Albus would begin his first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a> Ginny was the sports editor for the <i>Daily Prophet</i>, while her husband was promoted to Head of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a>. By this time all three of the couple's children were attending Hogwarts. In the same year, she joined <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> going back in time to save <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> and thwart <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>'s evil plans.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/21st_century" title="21st century">21st century</a>, Ginny Weasley taught the Bat-Bogey Hex to members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who pursued an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> profession, in order to help address the results of the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> In addition, as a Quidditch Star, Ginny instructed them on body control techniques upon falling off a broom, which they applied to increase the amount of damage they can take.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>A lot of boys like her. Even you think she's good-looking, don't you Blaise, and we all know how hard you are to please!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Discussion of Ginny's physical appearance<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127043147" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="264" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20101127043147" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127043147" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20101127043147" decoding="async" width="200" height="264" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20101127043147" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth year</a>, age 16</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny was described as being an extremely pretty girl, who had the typical <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> traits: flaming red hair (which she wore in a long mane) and a freckled complexion. She was of light skin, a very petite stature, and bright brown eyes like her mother. When blushed, Ginny would go a shade of red that matched her hair. When in a highly emotional state, she was known to acquire a "<i>hard, blazing look</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was stated that due to her prettiness, Ginny was perfectly capable of attracting a certain amount of attention from boys. In 1996, <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> stated that "<i>a lot of boys like her</i>" and that even <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Zabini" title="Blaise Zabini">Blaise Zabini</a> found her "good-looking", with the additional observation that he was very hard to please when it came to the physical appearance of women. Though Blaise immediately objected to this accusation, it could still count as a testament of sorts to Ginny's beauty. <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> also stated that she was very pretty during <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>'s wedding in 1997.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>You don't know how weird it is for her to be this shy, she never shuts up normally —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> regarding his sister's personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/File:Ginny_shy.gif" target="_blank"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="COS shy Ginny running away.gif" data-image-key="COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141208132824" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/File:Ginny_shy.gif" target="_blank"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141208132824" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="COS shy Ginny running away.gif" data-image-key="COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141208132824" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:COS_shy_Ginny_running_away.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny's shyness around Harry Potter, whom she has feelings for</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Ginny was a forceful, independent girl who often knew her own mind. She had an energetic, lively personality. Ginny also was known to be quick-witted, funny, and could often make others laugh even when they were feeling down.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> However, when she was young and in love with Harry in the early years of their friendship, she became shy and withdrawn in his presence.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> On the advice of their friend Hermione, she overcame it. She relaxed and reasserted her usual self, which was when he finally started noticing her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> One of the traits he was attracted to was that Ginny rarely got weepy.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny was popular during their time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and was fancied by numerous boys. Her brothers: <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, often thought that she was too popular for her own good. However, Ginny was good at lying and capable of being opaque when necessary. While staying at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>, she was taught by <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> how to check if a door had been imperturbed by flicking <a href="/wiki/Dungbomb" title="Dungbomb">dungbombs</a> at it and watching them bounce away as if hitting an invisible wall. When asked by her mother who was responsible, she blamed it on <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a>, even though her hands were filthy at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>Bet you loved that, didn’t you, Potter? Famous Harry Potter,” Can’t even go into a bookshop without making the front page.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Leave him alone, he didn't want all that!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny defending Harry against school bully Draco Malfoy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/File:Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif" target="_blank"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny standing up to Malfoy.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150716165528" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/File:Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif" target="_blank"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150716165528" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny standing up to Malfoy.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150716165528" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_standing_up_to_Malfoy.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny standing up to Draco Malfoy in Harry Potter's defence</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Growing up with six older brothers toughened her up. Ginny was not afraid to stand up to anybody, friends and foes alike. Notably, she stood up to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> on their first meeting in <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a> when he insulted Harry in 1992.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She even stood up to Hermione in defence of Harry's use of the <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, Ginny could be harsh towards those whom she disliked. For instance, she made fun of <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> behind her back when she first became engaged to <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>. She also <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">hexed</a> and crashed into <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a> when he irritated and insulted her on two separate occasions during her fifth year.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny was notably difficult to intimidate or frighten, as seen during her moments of standing up to Harry during his moments of rage and anger. This is particularly impressive given that Harry's rages were capable of terrifying even his best friends Ron and Hermione, who were both incredibly courageous individuals. Her courage enabled her to take part in a three-way duel alongside Luna and Hermione against the powerful and insane <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>.
</p><p>Ginny was an animal lover, especially fond of cats. When <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a> was petrified in her first year at Hogwarts, her brothers put her shock down to this fact, not knowing that Ginny was scared because she couldn't remember what she was doing at the time and feared that she was responsible.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She named Ron's owl "<i><a href="/wiki/Pigwidgeon" title="Pigwidgeon">Pigwidgeon</a></i>",<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and was known to be able to lure Crookshanks out of hiding to play with her when she wanted.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> In her fifth year, she finally got her own pet, a purple <a href="/wiki/Pygmy_Puff" title="Pygmy Puff">Pygmy Puff</a> from <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a> that she named <a href="/wiki/Arnold" title="Arnold">Arnold</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/92/Horse_Patronus.png/revision/latest?cb=20170109005249" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="170" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Horse Patronus.png" data-image-key="Horse_Patronus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/92/Horse_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170109005249" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/92/Horse_Patronus.png/revision/latest?cb=20170109005249" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/92/Horse_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170109005249" decoding="async" width="250" height="170" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Horse Patronus.png" data-image-key="Horse_Patronus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/92/Horse_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170109005249" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Horse_Patronus.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny's corporeal horse <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>, which she was able to conjure at age fourteen</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Come on, Ginny's not bad. Actually, I dunno how she got so good, seeing how we never let her play with us</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny's impressive Quidditch skills<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Ginny was a very powerful and talented <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>. She was also a naturally talented at the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts,</a> a gifted flyer and <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player. At the age of fourteen, she was able to conjure a corporeal Patronus — a very advanced piece of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> and proof of superior magical ability.<sup id="cite_ref-PM2_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM2-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Despite being often prevented from participating in combat by her mother mainly for her young age, Ginny was a highly talented and competent duellist. She had an uncanny ability for dodging her opponents' curses due to her agility and reflexes. Ginny survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> with only a minor injury.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She also fought <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> again during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and emerged unscathed. This was partly due to the use of <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a> and partly due to her agility.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> She later defended herself from a Death Eater during the <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_the_Burrow" title="Attack at the Burrow">Attack at the Burrow</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Ginny fired well-aimed <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a> into the crowd of attacking <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. She, Hermione, and Luna also held their own against <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, an extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark witch</a>. She managed to miss a Killing Curse by an inch, showing the remarkable prowess she possessed in <a href="/wiki/Martial_magic" title="Martial magic">martial magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
