<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408215540" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny casting Reducto.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408215540" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408215540" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408215540" decoding="async" width="245" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny casting Reducto.gif" data-image-key="Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408215540" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_casting_Reducto.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny casting <i>Reducto</i> during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: As a committed and enthusiastic member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Ginny learned how to successfully cast numerous defensive and offensive spells successfully, under <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s expert instruction. Ginny was capable of fighting numerous highly dangerous <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> throughout numerous battles of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, with her even surviving the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, showing her excellent defensive abilities.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Ginny was surprisingly skilful in dark magic and with the casting of <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a>. In particular the <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a>, which she was noted to be very adept with from a fairly young age. This even gained <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a>'s notice entirely for her "marvellous Bat-Bogey Hex".<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Ginny was capable of casting a very powerful and impressive <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">Reductor Curse</a>, which helped to distract Death Eaters once. She also was described to fire well-aimed <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxes</a> at her opponents.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Ginny was highly proficient in this branch of magic. In her first year, she animated <i>"a well card to sing shrilly when opened"</i>. She once used a single <a href="/wiki/Scouring_Charm" title="Scouring Charm">Scouring Charm</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> to clean all the <a href="/wiki/Stinksap" title="Stinksap">Stinksap</a> out of a compartment on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. She also had highly swift reflexes with the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>. Most impressively, at the age fourteen, she was able to cast the extremely advanced and powerful <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, which took the corporeal form of a <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">horse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OPF_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OPF-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png/revision/latest?cb=20161119004725" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="333" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley Quidditch Seeker.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119004725" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png/revision/latest?cb=20161119004725" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119004725" decoding="async" width="180" height="333" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley Quidditch Seeker.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119004725" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Weasley_Quidditch_Seeker.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her Quidditch uniform</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Ginny eventually became an accomplished flyer and played both <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a> (which she prefers, as she likes scoring goals) and <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>. Despite not playing Seeker regularly, she was able to defeat <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, a seasoned Seeker. She even effectively stepped into the shoes of the extremely talented <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> (although she admitted that Harry was a better Seeker than her), winning Gryffindor the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a> in 1996.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> As an adult, Ginny became a professional <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player for the <a href="/wiki/Holyhead_Harpies" title="Holyhead Harpies">Holyhead Harpies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_21-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> In later years, she used her experiences in the sport to instructed the new members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> on body control techniques upon falling off a broom.</li>
<li><b>Agility</b>: Ginny was small and extremely fast, making her adept at dodging spells in combat and flying to catch the Golden Snitch at Quidditch matches. However, she sometimes could be trapped, as one time a Death Eater grabbed Ginny by the ankle.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: At the young age of sixteen, Ginny was able to effectively co-lead <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> alongside <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, showing her to have been a capable and resilient leader.</li>
<li><b>Journalism</b>: As the Head Quidditch Correspondent for the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> following her retirement from professional Quidditch, Ginny has been shown in her articles to be a very fair and adept journalist and reporter, often composing very unbiased and accurate articles while still injecting a certain enthusiasm into her writing style. Her position as the head of this section of the Prophet shows her level of skill as a journalist and her level of responsibility while still remaining a celebrated reporter</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Ginny%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141208233945" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="175" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Ginny%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20141208233945" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Ginny%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141208233945" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Ginny%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20141208233945" decoding="async" width="175" height="175" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Ginny%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20141208233945" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny%27s_wand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny's wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginny_Weasley%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Ginny Weasley&#39;s wand">Wand</a></b>: Ginny's wand was made from <a href="/wiki/Yew" title="Yew">yew</a>, with an unknown length and <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>. Like most wizards and witches, she purchased it at <a href="/wiki/Ollivanders" title="Ollivanders">Ollivanders</a> before beginning her education at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Arnold" title="Arnold">Arnold</a></b>: Ginny's <a href="/wiki/Pygmy_Puff" title="Pygmy Puff">Pygmy Puff</a>, or miniature Puffskein, purchased from her brothers Fred and George Weasley at their shop, <a href="/wiki/Weasley%27s_Wizard_Wheezes" class="mw-redirect" title="Weasley&#39;s Wizard Wheezes">Weasley's Wizard Wheezes</a>, in August of 1996.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_Broom" class="mw-redirect" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s Broom">Broomstick</a></b>: Ginny had an unknown broom which she used for Quidditch as Chaser or Seeker.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">T. M. Riddle's Diary</a></b>: Tom Riddle's diary was in Ginny's possession before <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> destroyed in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> on 29 May, 1993. The memory that resided in the diary had begun <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">possessing</a> and slowly draining the life out of Ginny.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_coin" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army coin">Dumbledore's Army coin</a></b>: Each member of the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> had a coin that had numerals that changed into the time and date of the next meeting of the D.A. whenever the master coin (owned by Harry Potter) was changed. The coin would also warm up to alert the holder to the change.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_bedroom" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s bedroom">Bedroom</a></b>: Ginny's bedroom was where she used to sleep at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a>. It is located on the first floor landing. It was described as small, but bright. It also overlooking the family's orchard and was decorated with posters of the <a href="/wiki/Weird_Sisters" title="Weird Sisters">Weird Sisters</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gwenog_Jones" title="Gwenog Jones">Gwenog Jones</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Weasley_jumper" title="Weasley jumper">Weasley jumper</a></b>: As a member of the Weasley family she owned several Weasley Jumpers. They were made by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> for family and friends and sent as Christmas gifts.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_dress_robes" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s dress robes">Yule Ball robes</a></b>: Ginny wore dress robes to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in 1994. She was accompanied to the ball by <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_robes_to_Slughorn%27s_Christmas_party" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s robes to Slughorn&#39;s Christmas party">Dress robes</a></b>: These were the dress robes worn by Ginny to the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Slug Club Christmas party</a> on 20 December, 1996.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley%27s_bridesmaid_dress" title="Ginevra Weasley&#39;s bridesmaid dress">Bridesmaid's dress</a></b>: This was the dress Ginny wore to Bill and Fleur's wedding. She was a bridesmaid along with <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur</a>'s younger sister <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Delacour" title="Gabrielle Delacour">Gabrielle</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Weasleys">The Weasleys</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Weasleys">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: The Weasleys"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Well, you seemed too busy to call him a prat, and I thought someone should.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny regarding her brother <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny's relationship with her family was a good one, having been raised in a loving environment. She would often comfort them (especially her mother) in times of need. The only and long-waited daughter in the family, she had to deal with an over-protective mother, who tried to prevent Ginny from war meetings and in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, despite her previous displays of power and skill fighting alongside <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>. Nevertheless, she often helped her mother at housework and in tending wounded at hard times.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150828155323" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH promo headshot Bill Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150828155323" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150828155323" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150828155323" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH promo headshot Bill Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150828155323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH_promo_headshot_Bill_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bill, her oldest brother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny appeared to worship her brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>, defending his choice of earring and hairstyle to their mother,<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and initially feeling that he could do a lot better than <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, whom she mockingly called "<i>Phlegm</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>  She was in shock but helped to take care of Bill when he was permanently scarred by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Ginny got on well with <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, but found <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> to be a little overbearing and stuffy. She caught him kissing his girlfriend, <a href="/wiki/Penelope_Clearwater" title="Penelope Clearwater">Penelope Clearwater</a>, during her first year at Hogwarts, and proceeded to tell her other brothers about it after her recovery from possession by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Marvolo Riddle</a>'s memory.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Following Percy's decision to turn his back on his family over their support of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> instead of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>, Ginny was furious with him and even threw mashed parsnips at him when he came to the<a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow"> Burrow</a> at Christmas in 1996.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> .
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Just because he's never snogged anyone in his life, just because the best kiss he's ever had is from our Auntie Muriel —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Shut your mouth!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>No, I will not! I've seen you with <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Phlegm</a>, hoping she'll kiss you on the cheek every time you see her, it's pathetic! If you went out and got a bit of snogging done yourself, you wouldn't mind so much that everyone else does it!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny and Ron have an intense row in 1996<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140627001739" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo Fred Ron Ginny George.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140627001739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140627001739" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140627001739" decoding="async" width="250" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo Fred Ron Ginny George.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140627001739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_Fred_Ron_Ginny_George.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny with Fred, George, and Ron</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Percy tried to be a role model for Ginny and Ron, but the two youngest siblings took after Fred and George, the fun-loving twins. In temperament, she resembled the twins, <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George</a>, and, like them, often teased Ron, who was closest to her in age. Some of Ginny's brothers had difficulty accepting that their little sister was popular with the opposite gender; Ginny and Ron had a particularly nasty row after Ron caught her snogging <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, though they eventually made up.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Ginny has something of a love-hate relationship with Ron, while she loves him as a brother very much and cares deeply for him, their fights are usually quite ferocious. She had no problem telling Ron off when she believed his behaviour was unreasonable and no issues with embarrassing him in public, as when she openly mocked him for his crush on Fleur and even tripped him in front of her.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>  In 1994, Ginny comforted Ron when he humiliated himself by asking Fleur Delacour to attend the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with him, while still managing to find the situation very funny. In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> she and Ron had an vicious fight about Ginny kissing her boyfriend in public, it went as far as both siblings using wands and reducing Ginny to tears, something she hardly resorted to. Ron fired a <a href="/wiki/Hex" title="Hex">hex</a> right at Ginny but missed and if Harry had not interfered, Ginny would have retaliated.
</p><p>Ginny had a humourous side and makes many jokes to keep people's spirits up very much like Fred and George; however, her relationship with them was not perfect. She got angry with them for questioning her on her dating life and while they respected her relationship with Harry, they were not above finding ways to tease them about it. She was heartbroken by the death of her brother Fred during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Accio Quote!">"<i>Harry and Ginny are real soulmates. They're both very strong and very passionate. That's their connection, and they're remarkable together.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> expands on Harry and Ginny's romance<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Accio_Quote!" title="Accio Quote!">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>: Future husband, father of her children, and the love of her life</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Simply put, Harry Potter was the <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> of Ginny's life. At age ten, she only briefly made his acquaintance when he boarded the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> with her brother Ron. She developed a crush on him nonetheless when he visited the Burrow.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_8-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Shy and clumsy around him, Ginny confided her feelings in <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">Tom Riddle's Diary</a>. Her outpouring of emotions enabled Riddle's memory to take control of her. Harry eventually saved her life in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> by slaying <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Salazar Slytherin's Basilisk</a> with <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a> and destroying the diary with one of the serpent's fangs.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Harry saving her life served to make her more withdrawn when in his presence, barely able to speak in front of him.<sup id="cite_ref-PA_14-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>  She even sent him a singing card on Valentine's Day. 
</p><p>Meanwhile, Harry was friendly toward Ginny, but did not return her romantic feelings. When Ginny was in third year Ron suggested that Harry take her to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, but as it turned out she already had a date. Harry, given his purely platonic interest in Ginny at the time, was not upset by this. However, Ginny was "extremely miserable" and left the common room with her head bowed, upset at the knowledge that she could have gone to the ball with her long-time crush. Ginny sought advice from <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who suggested that she relax in front of Harry, be true to herself, and possibly even date other boys.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Taking this advice, Ginny dated both <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a><sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a> in her fourth and fifth years. Even though she dated other boys, Ginny never completely gave up on the hope that Harry would reciprocate her affections.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny would often defend Harry whenever she felt it was needed, such as; in 1992 when she stood up to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> and fiercely told him "<i>to leave [Harry] alone</i>". She also told off <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Zabini" title="Blaise Zabini">Blaise Zabini</a> in 1996 when he insulted Harry and even stood up to Hermione, her close personal friend in defence of his use of the <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse on Malfoy. In 1997 she told off her then boyfriend <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a> for laughing at the fact that Harry was injured by <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a> during a Quidditch match. On 11 July 2014, <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> remarked that Harry was "<i>publicity-hungry</i>" just as Ginny was approaching, and was subsequently taken "unaccountably ill" with what some called "<i>a jinx to the solar plexus</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-the-qwc2014-final_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-the-qwc2014-final-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Ginny was also somewhat possessive of Harry. She was visibly displeased with the attention <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Delacour" title="Gabrielle Delacour">Gabrielle Delacour</a> paid him, and spoke up when Harry's ex-girlfriend, <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, volunteered to take Harry to see <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Rowena Ravenclaw's Diadem</a>, insisting that <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> take Harry instead. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190119042316" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Harry and Ginny pre-kiss.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190119042316" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190119042316" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190119042316" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Harry and Ginny pre-kiss.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190119042316" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_HQ_still_Harry_and_Ginny_pre-kiss.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny gives Harry his seventeenth birthday present</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In Ginny's fifth year, Harry started to fall in love with her as well. His feelings had presumably been developing since the previous year. She had reasserted herself as a vibrant, witty, and independent young woman, rather than an awkward and shy little girl. They had a lot in common — both played <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>, both had suffered at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, and both showed great strength in <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">defensive and offensive magic</a>. Both have also fought alongside one another on a number of occasions. In the beginning of the year, Harry was slightly disappointed when, after a summer together, he remembered that Ginny did not normally hang around the <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">trio</a> at school. However, he did not realise the scope of his feelings for her until he and Ron ran into Ginny and Dean kissing. After witnessing them kissing, he frequently hoped that Dean and Ginny would break up.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I never really gave up on you. Not really. I always hoped.... Hermione told me to get on with life, maybe go out with some other people, relax a bit around you, because I never used to be able to talk if you were in the room, remember? And she thought you might take a bit more notice if I was a bit more — myself.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;How Ginny never got over her feelings for Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>By the end of her fifth year, Ginny and Harry began dating after spontaneously kissing in the aftermath of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> winning the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a>. They broke up shortly thereafter, as Harry realised that if they continued dating openly, Voldemort would seek to use her to get to him, as he had done previously. He simply could not bring himself to endanger her life while he sought a way to destroy Voldemort. Calling the break up an "act of nobility", Ginny accepted his decision, but always held onto the hope that he would return to her.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In spite of the break-up, their feelings for each other remained as strong as ever. On <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_seventeenth_birthday" title="Harry Potter&#39;s seventeenth birthday">Harry's seventeenth birthday</a>, Ginny "<i>kissed him as she had never kissed him before</i>," though they were interrupted by Ron, with Hermione in tow. Ron discouraged Harry from "<i>getting [Ginny's] hopes up</i>," mentioning that his sister was "<i>really cut up</i>" when Harry attempted to end their relationship. Hermione, on the other hand, seemed to be more sympathetic toward Harry and Ginny's actions.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140704030548" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry &amp; Ginny kiss.gif" data-image-key="Harry_&amp;_Ginny_kiss.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704030548" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140704030548" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704030548" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry &amp; Ginny kiss.gif" data-image-key="Harry_&amp;_Ginny_kiss.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140704030548" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_%26_Ginny_kiss.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Ginny express their love for each other during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While hunting for <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, Harry would stare at her dot on the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> for hours, hoping that she could somehow sense that he was watching over her. At school, Ginny participated in and helped lead an underground rebellion, during which she, Neville, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a> even attempted to steal <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a> from the Headmaster's office. They had heard that it was left to Harry in Dumbledore's will, and guessed that he needed it.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Harry and Ginny next saw each other shortly before the Battle of Hogwarts. 
</p><p>When the battle began, Harry wanted Ginny to stay out of the fighting, but was forced to ask her to leave the safety of the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> when he, Hermione, and Ron searched it for Ravenclaw's Diadem. As Harry prepared to be killed by Voldemort, he thought of Ginny, "<i>her blazing looks, and the feel of her lips on his.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> When it seemed that Harry had been murdered by Voldemort, Ginny was beyond heartbroken and screamed louder than anyone. The supposed death of her one love was enough to drive Ginny to attack the incredibly powerful <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> alongside Luna and Hermione. When the battle was over she was one of the first ones that rushed to hug Harry.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905045007" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Cursed Child – Harry &amp; Ginny.jpg" data-image-key="Cursed_Child_–_Harry_&amp;_Ginny.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905045007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905045007" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905045007" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Cursed Child – Harry &amp; Ginny.jpg" data-image-key="Cursed_Child_–_Harry_&amp;_Ginny.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905045007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cursed_Child_%E2%80%93_Harry_%26_Ginny.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A 40 year old Harry's and a 39 year old Ginny's continuing love for one another</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny and Harry rekindled their romance in the aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> and were eventually married. The union produced three children: <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> All three of the couple's children were named in honour of family members, friends, and allies (most of whom they are named after are deceased). Their marriage is shown to be mature and understanding, Harry also affectionately calls Ginny "Gin", rather than her full name. It is also revealed that after the events in the Chamber of Secrets, people shut Ginny out of their lives, but Harry came to her and played a game of <a href="/wiki/Exploding_Snap" title="Exploding Snap">Exploding Snap</a>. Ginny claims that she also felt specific love from Harry since that day and that his love for her always made her feel stronger. The two made Ginny's brother Ron and his wife Hermione the godparents to their eldest son, and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> the godfather to their second son. They also have several nieces and nephews.
</p><p>Despite their affectionate and passionate marriage, Ginny retained her ability to put Harry in his place over his actions and behaviours, such as when she forbade him from entering Albus's room during his disappearance. 
</p><p>Ginny was also unable to look upon her husband when he disguised himself as Voldemort during the events of the Cursed Child. This shows how much she hated Voldemort and how much she loved her husband, to the point where watching him bear the appearance of the man who had stolen so much from both of them was too much for her.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Children">Children</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Children">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Children"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>He'll be all right.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny comforting her husband as Albus leaves for Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206011704" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="175" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s kids.png" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_kids.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141206011704" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206011704" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141206011704" decoding="async" width="250" height="175" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s kids.png" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_kids.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141206011704" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%27s_kids.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny's children (left to right): <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ginny had three children with Harry; two sons named James Sirius and Albus Severus, and a daughter named Lily Luna. 
</p><p>Lily looked like her mother and was jealous of her brothers, who were leaving for <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, exactly as her mother had been in 1991. Ginny comforted Albus (who physically resembled his father) when he was nervous about the possibility of being sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> house, and scolded James for teasing his brother. After James interrupted his cousin <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire</a> while she was kissing <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a>, Ginny noted how similar he was to <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nieces_and_nephews">Nieces and nephews</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As Ginny had five brothers who survived the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, four of whom married at some point, she had quite a few nieces and nephews by <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>. Ginny's own children seemed closest to <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>'s children, whose son <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a> was the same age as Lily, and their daughter <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> was the same age as <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur</a>'s children were <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Weasley" title="Dominique Weasley">Dominique</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Louis_Weasley" title="Louis Weasley">Louis</a>; <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> and his wife, <a href="/wiki/Audrey_Weasley" title="Audrey Weasley">Audrey</a>, had <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley_II" title="Molly Weasley II">Molly</a> (named after her <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">paternal grandmother</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Lucy_Weasley" title="Lucy Weasley">Lucy</a>; <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> married <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a> and named their son <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley_II" title="Fred Weasley II">Fred</a> after George's <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">late twin brother</a>, while their daughter was called <a href="/wiki/Roxanne_Weasley" title="Roxanne Weasley">Roxanne</a>. When Ginny's son, James, discovered Victoire kissing Teddy Lupin at <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a>, he proceeded to interrupt them and then run back to his family to triumphantly announce what he'd seen, prompting Ginny to compare him to his Uncle Ron.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger">Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Hermione told me to get on with life, maybe go out with some other people, relax a bit around you, because I never used to be able to talk if you were in the room, remember? And she thought you might take a bit more notice if I was a bit more — myself.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Smart girl, that Hermione.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny regarding her confidence in Hermione and the advice given to her<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140628051648" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="309" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Granger Half Blood Prince.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140628051648" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140628051648" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140628051648" decoding="async" width="225" height="309" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Granger Half Blood Prince.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140628051648" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Granger_Half_Blood_Prince.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, a good friend and future sister-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione Granger was one of Ginny's best female friends and her confidante. Ginny was a year below Hermione in <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and they had become close by Ginny's second year; Hermione comforted Ginny that year when the presence of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> upset her (Ginny was more affected than most others due to her possession by Voldemort the previous year). Hermione stayed in Ginny's room during her frequent visits to <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> during summer vacations.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Ginny was the only one that Hermione confided in when <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> asked her to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and the only one who knew that she had kissed him at least once.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Ginny also told Hermione about her teaching herself how to fly and about her relationship with <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a> before her family and most others were aware of either.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hermione gave Ginny advice on how to deal with her feelings for Harry<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> — advice that would lead to her going out with him and their eventual marriage. In the summer of 1996, when Hermione was staying at the Burrow, Ginny and Hermione openly disliked <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> and criticised her together. Ginny appeared to be disgusted with her brother <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, Hermione's love interest, when, after a fight with Ginny, Ron began dating <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>. However, Ginny was not afraid to stand up to Hermione when she felt she was wrong, for example when Hermione scolded <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> for using the <i>Sectumsempra</i> spell.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two became sisters-in-law upon Hermione's marriage to Ron, and Hermione is the godmother of Ginny's <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">oldest child</a>. Ginny also had a niece, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose Weasley</a> and a nephew, <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo Weasley</a>, through Hermione's marriage to Ron.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fleur_Delacour">Fleur Delacour</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Molly Weasley</b>: "<i>...Bill and Fleur... well... What have they really got in common? He's a hard-working down-to-earth sort of person, whereas she's —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>A cow.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny's obvious dislike of Fleur's personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="300" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222230" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222230" decoding="async" width="225" height="300" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222230" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fleur_Delacour.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, her sister-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny did not care much for Fleur Delacour when she first arrived at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> in 1994. She found Fleur humourless and irritating, as she was given to complaining loudly about what she perceived as Hogwarts' many faults. Fleur often compared the school unfavourably to <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a>. Ginny teased <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> for his schoolboy crush on her. She also disapproved of Fleur's engagement to her eldest brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>, whom Ginny looked up to.
</p><p>Much to Ginny's displeasure, Bill sent Fleur to live with the Weasley family for a few days. During that time Ginny took to mockingly referring to Fleur as "<i>Phlegm,</i>" and complained about Fleur's tendency to patronise her. However, when Bill became permanently disfigured by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> and Fleur indignantly defended her husband's bravery, Ginny began to recognise Fleur's admirable qualities. The two eventually got along well, and Ginny even became a bridesmaid for her wedding.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ginny had two nieces and a nephew through Fleur's marriage to Bill.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Neville Longbottom</b>: "<i>I'm nobody.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>No, you're not.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny defending Neville against himself<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="350" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140610141612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140610141612" decoding="async" width="225" height="350" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20140610141612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, a good friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville asked Ginny to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> after he was turned down by Hermione, who had already agreed to go with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, and the two attended together as friends. When Ron suggested that she go to the ball with Harry, who had yet to find a date, she was disappointed at having missed a chance to go with him, but remained faithful to her agreement with Neville.<sup id="cite_ref-GF_24-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Ginny defended Neville when others laughed at him, and told him not to put himself down when he described himself as "nobody."<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She was also quite horrified when she heard that Neville's parents, <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank Longbottom</a>, had been <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">tortured</a> into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and become permanent residents of <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>.
</p><p>Ginny was among the friends who likely contributed to Neville gradually gaining confidence and courage, and, along with Luna Lovegood, the two of them maintained the strongest support of Dumbledore's Army throughout the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. She and Harry remained close friends with Neville in their later years, as Ginny asked her son, James Sirius, to "<i>give Neville their love</i>" when Neville taught James <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Luna_Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Ginny's been nice though, she stopped two boys from calling me "</i>Loony<i>" the other day...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Luna's positive opinion of Ginny<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220801" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luna Lovegood profile Deathly Hallows.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220801" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220801" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220801" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luna Lovegood profile Deathly Hallows.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220801" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, a close friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny was friendly with Luna Lovegood, a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> student in her year, although the two did not grow close until they were both members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> in their fourth year. Ginny referred to Luna as "<i>Loony Lovegood</i>" just before introducing her to Harry and Neville in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, but soon stood up to those who ridiculed Luna.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In return, Luna genuinely appreciated Ginny's friendship; she once mentioned how much she liked Ginny while commentating on a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>-<a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match in which Ginny was playing <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ginny was also one of the five portraits — along with Harry, Ron, Hermione , and Neville — that Luna painted and hung from her bedroom ceiling, with the message "<i>friends</i>" joining them together in gold writing.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Luna may be one of Ginny's best female friends (along with Hermione), as Ginny was only seen with these girls during her school years. Ginny later gave her daughter <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily</a> the middle name "Luna", implying that the two remained very close well into adulthood.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nymphadora_Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I'd much rather have Tonks in the family. At least she's a laugh.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny's sisterly friendship with Tonks<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="300" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222048" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222048" decoding="async" width="225" height="300" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20161119222048" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, her friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny met Nymphadora Tonks in the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> through the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, and she and Hermione immediately struck up a friendship with the young <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>. Ginny appreciated that Tonks, although an adult, was interested in having fun. She taught Ginny how to check if a door had an <a href="/wiki/Imperturbable_Charm" title="Imperturbable Charm">Imperturbable Charm</a> on it by flicking <a href="/wiki/Dungbomb" title="Dungbomb">Dungbombs</a> at it. She also entertained Ginny and Hermione by displaying her <a href="/wiki/Metamorphmagus" title="Metamorphmagus">Metamorphmagus</a> abilities, usually at the dinner table.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Ginny hoped her brother, Bill, would choose Tonks over <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> — an idea Ron seemed to find laughable. After Tonks was murdered by her own aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Ginny duelled Bellatrix, along with Hermione and Luna, although it is unknown if Ginny knew that it was Bellatrix who had murdered Tonks. After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ginny and her children were very close to <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy</a>, the son of Tonks and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black">Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Excuse me, but I care what happens to Sirius as much as you do!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ginny regarding her liking of Sirius<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
