<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="336" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20150918055024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20150918055024" decoding="async" width="225" height="336" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20150918055024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, her friend and husband's godfather</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though Ginny first learned of Sirius in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> as an <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> escapee convicted of killing 12 muggles, she was soon made aware of his innocence through her connections to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and his godson, Harry. She and Sirius grew closer during their mutual time spent at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">the Order's headquarters</a>, and she later told Harry that she cared about Sirius as much as he did, insisting on accompanying Harry to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, where they believed Sirius was being held and tortured by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. When Sirius and four other members of the Order arrived at the Ministry to rescue Ginny and her friends, who had walked into a trap and been attacked by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, Sirius was murdered by his cousin, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>.
</p><p>Harry and Ginny were both horribly saddened by Sirius's death, and later duelled Bellatrix in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Ginny married Sirius's godson later and she and Harry gave their eldest son <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James</a> the middle name "Sirius" in honour of him.
</p>
<h3><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Cho Chang</b>: "<i>The Defence Association? The DA for short, so nobody knows what we're talking about?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Yeah, the DA's good. Only let's make it stand for Dumbledore's Army, because that's the Ministry's worst fear, isn't it?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Cho and Ginny trying to find a name for Dumbledore's Army<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, her friends and allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's Army was an organisation founded by Harry Potter, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> in 1995, and led and taught by Harry Potter to oppose <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, as well as offer students a place to learn and practise <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">defensive magic</a>. Ginny was one of the first to join, and the one who came up with calling the organisation "<i>Dumbledore's Army,</i>" based on <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>'s paranoid fears of Dumbledore mobilising Hogwarts students in a coup against the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>. She was also partially responsible for bringing several of its Ravenclaw members into the fold, as her then-boyfriend Michael Corner brought his friends <a href="/wiki/Terry_Boot" title="Terry Boot">Terry Boot</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Goldstein" title="Anthony Goldstein">Anthony Goldstein</a> with him to the first meeting.
</p><p>Ginny was on good terms with most of the D.A., making them laugh with her highly accurate impression of Umbridge's signature cough and generally proving to be a skilled duellist; the major exceptions to this would have been <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>, who betrayed the DA to Umbridge, and <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, whom Ginny once purposely crashed into after a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match, and who deserted the DA prior to the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Ginny also showed some wariness of Harry's ex-girlfriend, <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, when Cho wanted to take Harry to see <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Rowena Ravenclaw's Diadem</a>, insisting Luna take him instead. Ginny convinced her then boyfriend, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, and his friends to join, and the DA may have been where Ginny first became friendly with <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, whom she would date the next year.
</p><p>Ginny, along with Neville and Luna, co-led the DA in opposition to <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/1997%E2%80%931998_school_year" title="1997–1998 school year">1997–1998 school year</a>, writing slogans on walls and at one point attempting to steal the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> from Headmaster Snape's office.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cho_Chang">Cho Chang</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Cho Chang">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Cho Chang"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Cho Chang</b>: "<i>If you'd like to see what the diadem's supposed to look like, I could take you up to our common room and show you, Harry? Ravenclaw's wearing it in her statue</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>No, Luna will take Harry, won't you, Luna?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny's possessiveness regarding Harry and her mistrust of Cho<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161217054602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo Cho cropped.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161217054602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054602" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo Cho cropped.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_Cho_cropped.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, her <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">husband</a>'s ex-girlfriend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny always held an amount of jealousy toward Cho, as Cho was <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s first crush, girlfriend, and shared with Harry his first kiss. Despite this however, Ginny was considerate enough of her that after Harry and Cho had broken up, she eventually advised  Harry that things could be mended between them if he reached out to Cho  but then was interrupted by Harry clarifying that he actually wished to talk to his godfather Sirius, making this advice null and void. When Cho offered to take <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> common room so he could see the statue of <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">her diadem</a> briefly before the Battle of Hogwarts, Ginny cut across her and said that <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a> would take Harry to the common room instead, implying that she still felt somewhat threatened by Cho and her still present crush on Harry.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dean_Thomas">Dean Thomas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dean Thomas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Dean Thomas"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Just choose someone — better — next time.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Well, I've chosen Dean Thomas, would you say he's better?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and Ginny about the latter's relationships<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png/revision/latest?cb=20161124200524" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="239" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo Dean Thomas.png" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161124200524" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png/revision/latest?cb=20161124200524" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161124200524" decoding="async" width="180" height="239" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo Dean Thomas.png" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161124200524" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_Dean_Thomas.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, her ex-boyfriend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny started dating Dean Thomas at the end of her fourth year.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Ginny's brother and Dean's roommate <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> disapproved of the romance, as demonstrated by his furious reaction to stumbling upon the couple kissing passionately in a deserted hallway. They appeared to be very close at first, but, according to Ginny's friend <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, things began to get rocky as Ginny became displeased with Dean for what she perceived as over-protectiveness, as Dean constantly tried to assist her in everything. 
</p><p>Ginny's enthusiasm about the relationship seemed to ebb by <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a> of <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, as she did not seem terribly eager to see Dean upon her return to Hogwarts. The couple also began to row over little things, like Dean's constant attempts to help Ginny through the portrait hole into the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> common room, and they fought after Dean and <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus</a> laughed when Harry suffered a fractured skull courtesy of <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120220120435" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny and Dean drinking together.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120220120435" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120220120435" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120220120435" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny and Dean drinking together.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120220120435" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_and_Dean_drinking_together.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dean and Ginny on a date at the <a href="/wiki/Three_Broomsticks_Inn" title="Three Broomsticks Inn">Three Broomsticks</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry, under the influence of <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a>, actually ignited the minor argument that led to their breakup when he accidentally brushed past Ginny climbing through the portrait hole; as Harry was wearing his <a href="/wiki/Invisibility_cloak" title="Invisibility cloak">invisibility cloak</a>, Ginny thought Dean was once again attempting to help her, and snapped at him. Ginny clearly got over Dean soon after they broke up, as she began dating Harry soon after and admitted to him that she had never really given up on Harry. Dean took the break up much harder; he broke the glass he was holding upon witnessing Ginny and Harry's first kiss.<sup id="cite_ref-HP_12-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HP-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Michael_Corner">Michael Corner</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Michael Corner">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Michael Corner"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Michael — but — but you were going out with him!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny</b>: "<i>Not any more. He didn't like Gryffindor beating Ravenclaw at Quidditch and got really sulky, so I ditched him and he ran off to comfort Cho instead.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny on her break-up with Michael Corner<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Mikecorner.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20161123060928" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mikecorner.JPG" data-image-key="Mikecorner.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Mikecorner.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161123060928" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Mikecorner.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20161123060928" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Mikecorner.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161123060928" decoding="async" width="180" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mikecorner.JPG" data-image-key="Mikecorner.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Mikecorner.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161123060928" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mikecorner.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, her ex-boyfriend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny and Michael Corner met at the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, and began dating at the end of the school year, she used the relationship as an attempt to "move on" from Harry Potter. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, she brought him and some of his friends along to the first meeting of what would become <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. When the two duelled during meetings, Michael did not hit Ginny with anything, possibly because she was his girlfriend. When Michael drew unnecessary attention to the D.A. at one point, Ginny called him a "<i>fool</i>", though not to his face.
</p><p>Ginny ended the relationship on the basis of Michael being a "<i>bad loser</i>," following Michael's poor reaction to Gryffindor beating Ravenclaw in a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match.<sup id="cite_ref-OP_15-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Michael went on to date <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, who, like Ginny, also had a romance with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140618165730" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="260" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin profile 2.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140618165730" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140618165730" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140618165730" decoding="async" width="180" height="260" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin profile 2.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140618165730" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_profile_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, her former DADA professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus Lupin was Ginny's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher during her second year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Lupin comforted Ginny after her first encounter with <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> by giving her a piece of chocolate, and she likely believed, along with many other Hogwarts students, that he made an excellent teacher. Ginny and Remus met again in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, at 12 Grimmauld Place, and several times after that, as Remus was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and good friends with Ginny's parents. Ginny was thrilled when he married <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, and remained close with their son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy</a>, well after Tonks and Remus were murdered during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>Ginny first met <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, the Hogwarts gamekeeper in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, during her first year at Hogwarts. Ginny seemed to be friendly with Hagrid, as they were both friends of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>. At one point, Hagrid told Harry that he saw Ginny near his <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">hut</a>; he supposed that Ginny hoped to see Harry, and teased Harry for it. After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Hagrid appeared to be friendly with <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>, the youngest son of Ginny and Harry.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, her former headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny, like many people, thought Albus Dumbledore was the greatest wizard of all time. Ginny met Dumbledore in 1992, during her first year at Hogwarts, where Dumbledore was Headmaster. Dumbledore comforted and reassured Ginny after she was possessed by a fragment of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s soul and manipulated into opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>. Ginny was one of the first people to learn about Dumbledore's death, and the only one able to console Harry afterwards. Ginny and Harry named her younger son after Dumbledore.
</p><p>Ginny also happened to like Minerva McGonagall, her <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> professor and Head of House. It is obvious that McGonagall could have been fond of Ginny since she was a talented witch and did not condone or tolerate bullying, something that McGonagall most likely valued.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, former DADA professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like nearly everyone else at Hogwarts, Ginny despised professor Dolores Umbridge, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">ministry</a>-appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor for the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>. Umbridge was a horrible sadistic witch who enjoyed torturing students for punishment with the use of a <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Blood Quill</a>, and attempted to take firm control of the school by passing a series of <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree" title="Educational Decree">Educational Decrees</a>. Ginny became a member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> in order to oppose her, as well to learn the practical defensive magic Umbridge refused to teach in class.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, her former positions and DADA teacher</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/1997-1998_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1997-1998 school year">1997-1998 school year</a>, Ginny, along with Neville Longbottom and Luna Lovegood, re-formed and co-led Dumbledore's Army in rebellion against then Headmaster Severus Snape and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who had been appointed professors at Hogwarts and enjoyed punishing students with the use of the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.
</p><p>Ginny showed particular dislike for the Potions master, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> as he was a cruel and very unpopular teacher. Aside from his creepy demeanour and snide attitude toward everyone, he had always favoured Slytherins because they were in his house and her particular dislike for Snape was something she shared with her brothers and friends. She also knew that he was part of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and when she learnt that Snape killed Dumbledore, she thought he had betrayed the Order. She was also, obviously, not happy about his tenure as Headmaster when Hogwarts fell under <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s control. However, near the end of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, she learnt from Harry that he was on their side all along. It is unknown how she acted to the revelation of Snape's true loyalties. She did allow her second son to have his middle name from Severus.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>...I was patient. I wrote back. I was sympathetic, I was kind. Ginny simply </i>loved<i> me... "No one's ever understood me like you, Tom... I'm so glad I've got this diary to confide in... It's like a friend I can carry around in my pocket..." If I say it myself, Harry, I've always been able to charm the people I needed.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom Riddle regarding his manipulation of Ginny<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706215126" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle (16 years old).jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706215126" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle (16 years old).jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, her enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> got into a fistfight with <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a> prior to the start of Ginny's first year, Malfoy used the opportunity to slip <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s diary">Tom Riddle's diary</a> into the pile of books Ginny was carrying. Though Malfoy most likely believed the diary was simply enchanted to open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, it was actually one of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, and in fact, contained a fragment of the Dark Lord's soul.
</p><p>Tom Riddle's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> communicated with Ginny through his diary, sympathising with her problems and giving her advice, which made her emotionally vulnerable to Riddle's influence. Eventually, Riddle was able to possess Ginny, use her to open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, and free <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Salazar Slytherin's Basilisk</a> to petrify several <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students (including <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>). Ginny eventually figured out what she had been doing, despite having no memory of what happened during the times she was possessed, after finding herself covered in feathers and rooster blood. She attempted to flush the diary down a toilet, but being a Horcrux, it remained undamaged and later ended up in the hands of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.
</p><p>Ginny, worried the diary would reveal to Harry things she'd written about <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">her feelings for him</a>, stole the diary back. Riddle possessed Ginny one last time and had her enter the Chamber of Secrets, with every intention of killing her and using her life to restore his own. Harry, however, as a <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouth</a>, was able to enter the Chamber, rescue Ginny, and slay the Basilisk with the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a>. He then used one of the Basilisk's fangs to stab the diary, effectively making it the first of Voldemort's Horcruxes to be destroyed.
</p><p>Upon speaking with Dumbledore about the diary's remains, Ginny and her family came to learn that Tom Riddle is the original name of Lord Voldemort, much to Ginny's horror. According to herself in later years, Ginny would never forget these experiences and comforted Harry when he thought he was suffering a similar experience.
</p><p>Upon time travelling to the night of her parents-in-law's murder, Ginny was horrified by her husband's transfiguration into an exact duplicate of Voldemort, showing that she still despised him passionately. In her words, she couldn't stand to see the man she loved in the face of the man she hated.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Media"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Ginevra is the Italian form of the name <i>Guinevere</i>, which means "fair one". <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guinevere" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Guinevere">Guinevere</a> is also the name of King Arthur's wife in Arthurian legend, famous for her affair with Arthur's chief knight Sir Lancelot. There seems to be a pattern in the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> of naming members after characters in Arthurian legend. Another famous muse bearing this name was <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ginevra_King" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ginevra King">Ginevra King</a>, a socialite who inspired <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F._Scott_Fitzgerald" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:F. Scott Fitzgerald">F. Scott Fitzgerald</a>'s character Daisy Buchanan in <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Great_Gatsby" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Great Gatsby">The Great Gatsby</a></i>. The name <i>Ginevra</i> is also an Italian variant of <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Juniper_(given_name)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Juniper (given name)">Juniper</a></i>, derived from the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Juniper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Juniper">tree or berry</a>. Junipers were often used to represent chastity in Renaissance-period art, such as in Leonardo da Vinci's <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ginevra_de%27_Benci" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ginevra de&#39; Benci">Ginevra de' Benci</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> With links to the Welsh and Celtic history, Ginevra also means virgin. In some cultures, Ginevra can mean "white shadow, or white wave".
</p><p>Ginny's married name is <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Potter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Potter">Potter</a>, a very common surname of English origin.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> It traditionally refers to the occupation of making pottery. <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beatrix_Potter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Beatrix Potter">Beatrix Potter</a> was a well-known English children's author. <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Potter%27s_Field" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Potter&#39;s Field">Potter's Field</a> is the name for a burial ground for the unknown or unclaimed dead, particularly soldiers and orphans; the Potter family had many members that fit that description. The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Potter_Box" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Potter Box">Potter Box</a> is a model for making ethical decisions developed at Harvard University. <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has also commented that she has liked the name since childhood, as a family that had lived near her carried this surname.<sup id="cite_ref-accio-quote.org2_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-accio-quote.org2-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160725210424" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="281" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg" data-image-key="Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160725210424" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160725210424" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160725210424" decoding="async" width="180" height="281" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg" data-image-key="Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3f/Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160725210424" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hbp.c25-the-seer-overheard.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny as portrayed in the chapter art of the Half-Blood Prince</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070222175127" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="256" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="GOF promo casual wear Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070222175127" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070222175127" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070222175127" decoding="async" width="180" height="256" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="GOF promo casual wear Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070222175127" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:GOF_promo_casual_wear_Ginny_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bonnie_Wright" title="Bonnie Wright">Bonnie Wright</a> as Ginny Weasley</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/GinnyWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200716115338" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="485" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="GinnyWU.png" data-image-key="GinnyWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/GinnyWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200716115338" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/GinnyWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200716115338" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/GinnyWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200716115338" decoding="async" width="180" height="485" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="GinnyWU.png" data-image-key="GinnyWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/GinnyWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200716115338" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:GinnyWU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny Weasley as she appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>It is stated that Ginny looked forward to attending Hogwarts, ever since Bill began attending,<sup id="cite_ref-CS_7-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> however since Bill began attending in 1982, when Ginny was only a year old, this seems unlikely as she would have been too young to realise what was going on. It is more likely that one of her earliest memories, likely from the age of three or four, would be of both Bill and Charlie heading off to school.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and Ginny share a lot in common when it comes to Lord Voldemort-they were both temporary <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouths</a>, they were both briefly possessed by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and they have also lost family members to Voldemort.</li>
<li>According to Harry Potter, her most attractive feature is her red hair.</li>
<li>Ginny is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actress <a href="/wiki/Bonnie_Wright" title="Bonnie Wright">Bonnie Wright</a> in all of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a>, making her one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations.
<ul><li>Wright has also provided the voice for Ginny in the video game versions of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (video game)">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (video game)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bonnie_Wright" title="Bonnie Wright">Bonnie Wright</a> has blue eyes, instead of brown, as Ginny is described as having. She is also not as short as Ginny is described to be in the books.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bonnie_Wright" title="Bonnie Wright">Bonnie Wright</a>'s favourite Ginny Weasley quote was "Good luck."</li>
<li>Ginny's role is shortened early on in the films. She has very few lines and only a few minutes worth of screen time in <i>Chamber of Secrets</i>. She only has one line and has not even one minute of screen time in <i>Prisoner of Azkaban</i>. Again, in <i>Goblet of Fire</i>, she has a very small role.</li></ul></li>
<li>Ginny is portrayed by British actress <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Miller" title="Poppy Miller">Poppy Miller</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child_(play)#Original_West_End_production" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child (play)">original West End production</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-cast1_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cast1-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Ginny is voiced by Imogen Church in the audiobook version of <i><a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Through_the_Ages_(real)" title="Quidditch Through the Ages (real)">Quidditch Through the Ages (real)</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Ginny wears the number 5 in her <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> tunic in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>. Many photographs and posters have her wearing number 6, but that is the number of the generic tunic she wore only for the try-outs.</li>
<li>Ginny's <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> is a <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">horse</a>. It is never described in the books, but is shown in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>. This was later confirmed by <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>.</li>
<li>In the film adaptations, Ginny's relationship with <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a> was cut. However, it is included in the video game of the film.</li>
<li>J.K. Rowling has stated that she had planned certain moments, such as Ginny beating <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Golden Snitch</a> during a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match, from the start as a subtle comparison between Ginny and Cho, showing that Ginny was a better match for Harry.</li>
<li>Many fans believed that "Ginny" was short for "Virginia." It was later established that Ginny's given name is "Ginevra", as her Great Aunt Muriel referred to her as such during Bill and Fleur's wedding in Deathly Hallows.</li>
<li>Several times throughout the series, some of Ginny's actions are described as being catlike. However, her personality does not reflect the style of her actions, as her <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> is a horse instead of a cat.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> revealed a <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="https://pbs.twimg.com/media/CgUnAo9XEAEDd4-.jpg">picture</a> via her official Twitter account on <a href="/wiki/18_April" title="18 April">18 April</a>, <a href="/wiki/2016" title="2016">2016</a> showing her idea of some of the main character's wand designs, where Ginny's wand wood was revealed for the first time to be made from <a href="/wiki/Yew" title="Yew">yew</a>. Interestingly enough, both Harry Potter's wife and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">mortal enemy</a> share the same wand wood.</li>
<li>Ginny has two soundtracks which are titled as <i>Ginny</i> and <i>When Ginny Kissed Harry</i> on the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(soundtrack)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (soundtrack)">soundtrack</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>.</li>
<li>Ginny Weasley and Harry Potter's romantic relationship is told in a slightly different way in the films from the novels of <i>Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</i> and <i>Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</i> and <i>Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2:</i>
<ul><li>In the novel of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Harry shares his first kiss with Ginny in front of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students in the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Common_Room" title="Gryffindor Common Room">Gryffindor Common Room</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> won the Quidditch Cup. Also in the book, Harry ends his romantic relationship with Ginny at <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s funeral.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Ginny and Harry go to the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> together to hide the <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Half-Blood Prince's copy of Advanced Potion-Making</a>, after he curses <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. While there, Ginny asks Harry to close his eyes while she goes and hides the book so that he and other students cannot find it. When she returns to Harry, she kisses him. Harry was very much delighted and surprised that he received a kiss from Ginny. Also at the end of the film, it is implied that Ginny and Harry are still dating.</li>
<li>In the novel of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a></i>, Harry and Ginny kiss in Ginny's room in the Burrow and Ron interrupts them when he opens the door.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i>, Ginny comes down to the sitting room and asks Harry to help zip up her dress. Harry and Ginny then share a kiss that gets interrupted by George Weasley.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, Ginny and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> are both climbing up on one of the staircases, and run into <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> during the battle. <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville</a> ask Harry if he has seen <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">he</a> confesses to Ginny and Harry that he has feelings for <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">he</a> went away to find and tell <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>. Harry and Ginny share a quick kiss, Harry was going to tell Ginny that he loved her, but Ginny quickly told him that she knows, and they both went back to what they were doing before they met up. This did not happen in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i> book.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the book of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>, Ginny is wearing a golden dress at the <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour</a>. In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i>, she is spotted wearing a sliver and black dress at the <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a>.</li>
<li>In the LEGO Harry Potter series, Ginny's actions towards Harry are set out differently:<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20190911154945" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley LEGO HP1-4.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190911154945" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20190911154945" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190911154945" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley LEGO HP1-4.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190911154945" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Weasley_LEGO_HP1-4.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny Weasley in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In Year 2, when she sees Harry arrive, she sighs and giggles at the sight of him. At Flourish and Blotts, she shows no interest in Lockhart and instead attempts to attract Harry. In the Chamber of Secrets, she shows no sign of worry or fear about her own and many other's near deaths, but simply smiles lovingly at Harry, hearts appearing over her.</li>
<li>In Year 4, she seems more concerned over Harry's faint in the Quidditch World Cup than anyone.</li>
<li>In Year 5, she appears to be greatly disappointed over the obvious feelings between Harry and Cho and desperately tries to beat Cho to it, narrowly failing. In the Department of Mysteries, she seems reluctant to go with Luna and Neville rather than Harry. While Harry is being possessed, she rushes up to see the events first and affectionately strokes his arm at the end of the year.</li>
<li>In Year 6, her relationship with Dean is cut and she seems more devoted to Harry as ever, flirting with him at the Burrow and even in front of every one else in the Slug Club. She also appears to have taken Harry to the Room of Requirement simply for the opportunity to kiss Harry.</li>
<li>In Year 7: Part 2, she arrives at the room of Requirement to see Harry. They run towards each other to kiss, but stop and just shake hands awkwardly.</li>
<li>The fact that her relationship with Dean was cut in Year 6 makes it unknown why Harry and Ginny did not attend the Slug Club Christmas Party together. However, they are seen dating in the beginning of the "Slug Club" level after the first cutscene.</li></ul></li></ul>
<h3><span id="Author's_comments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Author.27s_comments">Author's comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>"<i>I think you can see that she is a fairly forceful personality (and she always has been, remember Ron saying that she 'never shuts up' in Chamber of Secrets)?"</i><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Da-ginny.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170627170030" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Da-ginny.jpg" data-image-key="Da-ginny.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Da-ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20170627170030" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Da-ginny.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170627170030" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Da-ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20170627170030" decoding="async" width="175" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Da-ginny.jpg" data-image-key="Da-ginny.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Da-ginny.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20170627170030" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Da-ginny.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny Weasley as depicted on  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>"<i>The plan was, which I really hope I fulfilled, is that the reader, like Harry, would gradually discover Ginny as pretty much the ideal girl for Harry. She's tough, not in an unpleasant way, but she's gutsy. He needs to be with someone who can stand the demands of being with Harry Potter, because he's a scary boyfriend in a lot of ways. He's a marked man. I think she's funny, and I think that she's very warm and compassionate. These are all things that Harry requires in his ideal woman. But, I felt — and I'm talking years ago when all this was planned — initially, she's terrified by his image. I mean, he's a bit of a rock god to her when she sees him first, at 10 or 11, and he's this famous boy. So Ginny had to go through a journey as well… I feel that Ginny and Harry, in this book, they are total equals. They are worthy of each other. They've both gone through a big emotional journey, and they've really got over a lot of delusions, to use your word, together. So, I enjoyed writing that. I really like Ginny as a character.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>"<i>The backstory with Ginny was, she was the first girl to arrive in the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> in generations, but there's that old tradition of the seventh daughter of a seventh daughter and a seventh son of a seventh son, so that's why she's the seventh, because she is a gifted witch. I think you get hints of that, because she does some pretty impressive stuff here and there, and you'll see that again.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>"<i>Harry and Ginny are real soul mates. They're both very strong and very passionate. That's their connection, and they're remarkable together</i>... <i>I think she's like Harry. He's got an intellectual curiosity and she's got something of belief.</i>"</li>
<li>"<i>Harry and Ginny were always meant to be together. I thought it was obvious, but apparently there were internet wars about this.</i>"</li></ul>
